注意：上述限度為建議值，各廠商應依據產品特性、風險評估及病患安全考量自行建立產品特定限度，且替代限度的合理性論述應文件化並納入法規申報。

本節重點回顧 Section Summary — Section 3

  • Proactive vs. Reactive 的根本差異：Proactive 在上市申請時即預先核准再處理方案，觸發時直接執行；Reactive 是事後因應，需要補充申請及額外的主管機關溝通，複雜步驟風險高，應盡量以 Proactive 設計取代。
  • Continuation ≠ Reprocessing：在批記錄預設範圍內的製程調整屬於「延續」，不需偏差申報；超出設計範圍才是「再處理」。正確分類是 GMP 合規的基礎，文件設計應消除灰色地帶。
  • 頻率管控雙維度：需同時監控「單批次再處理次數上限」（由驗證研究定義，例如 Dead-End Filtration 通常 max 3 次）及「批次間頻率」（APR/PQR 趨勢分析，示例性門檻 10%），兩者均超標代表製程失控。
  • 蛋白質聚集是首要品質風險：每次再處理都是額外的蛋白質壓力暴露，需評估黏度增加、熱應力、剪切力、氣液界面等因素。聚集體增加直接關聯免疫原性風險，危害患者安全。
  • 20 步驟框架是實作路線圖：從 FMEA 評估到法規申報，框架提供完整的前瞻性設計路徑，適用於商業化後及開發階段。關鍵節點：Step 4 觸發偵測時效性、Step 10 可比性標準建立、Step 18 CTD Module 對應（3.2.S.2.2/2.5/2.6）。
  • CCS 在再處理中的強化要求：再處理增加了微生物、內毒素、微粒污染的風險，需結合 QRM 和 CCS（PIC/S Annex 1 2022 要求），並對執行再處理的操作人員建立更嚴格的監控方案。無菌保證永遠是最高優先級（決策層級 #1）。
  • CDMO 核心提醒：在承接新產品時，應主動與 Sponsor 討論哪些步驟具有再處理需求，並在 IND/CTA 階段就規劃 Proactive 方案，避免商業化後的 Reactive 困境。TFDA 要求再處理批次放行前需取得主管機關核准，與 FDA 框架一致。
4

Section 4: Regulatory Framework

法規架構 | p23-p29

PDA Technical Report No. 74 (Revised 2026) | p23-p29

本章學習目標

  • 理解 ICH 指引如何協調各市場對 reprocessing/reworking 申報的共同要求
  • 區分 FDA 三層申報類別（PAS / CBE-30 / AR）及其適用情境
  • 掌握 EMA Variation Regulation 的三層類別（Type II / IB / IA）並與 FDA 類別對應
  • 辨識台灣 CDMO 服務全球 Sponsor 時，reprocessing 事件應觸發哪種申報動作
  • 了解 PIC/S、WHO、BioPhorum 等其他法規參考框架的定位
4.0 Introduction to the Regulatory Framework 法規架構導論

原文內容 Original Text

Guidelines published by ICH contain harmonized guidance specifically for to-be-marketed and marketed pharmaceuticals, including biologicals, specifically for submissions involving reprocessing of biologicals. Some of the common characteristics harmonized to enable efficient reprocessing submissions include:

  • To-Be-Marketed: Initial market application to contain details of any anticipated future reprocessing in the relevant sections of the Common Technical Document (CTD) referred to as a Post-Approval Change Management Protocol (PACMP). Allowing this inclusion of reprocessing protocols for relevant steps provides reprocessing flexibility and minimizes post-approval reporting.
  • Marketed: Post-market clear guidance and well-defined timeframes for review and approval of Post-Approval Changes (PAC), as well as PACMPs.
  • Acceptance of science- and risk-based approaches for developing data to support PACs and PACMPs.
  • Relatively fewer requests for additional documentation not included in CTD Module 3.

Table 4.2-1 provides guidance on reprocessing/reworking in the ICH guidelines.

"Allowing this inclusion of reprocessing protocols for relevant steps provides reprocessing flexibility and minimizes post-approval reporting."

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

PACMP (Post-Approval Change Management Protocol，上市後變更管理計畫)： 在初次申請上市許可（NDA/BLA/MAA）時，主動在 CTD 中預先聲明未來可能執行的 reprocessing 步驟及其可接受標準。審查機關預先審核後，日後若實際發生，僅需 Annual Report（AR）或 CBE 層級即可，而非 PAS。這是主動規劃、降低未來監管負擔的核心策略。

CTD（Common Technical Document，通用技術文件）：ICH M4 規範的全球統一申請格式，Module 3 為 CMC 資料，是 reprocessing 協議主要存放位置。

比喻說明 Analogy

PACMP 就像建築師在設計圖審查時，就先取得「未來改建預審許可」。房子蓋好後若按圖改建，不用再重新申請建照，只需備案。若未事先審查就擅自改建，則需完整重新審查（= PAS）。在生物製劑 reprocessing 上，這個時間差可能意味著數月甚至一年的延誤。

重點提示 Key Notes

ICH 協調框架的核心效益：同一套 PACMP 可同時支援 FDA BLA 及 EMA MAA 申請，大幅降低 CDMO 在多市場服務 Sponsor 時的文件重工量。台灣 TFDA 接受 PIC/S 標準，而 PIC/S 主要參照 EMA 架構——因此 PACMP 設計時應以 EMA 要求為基準，確認 FDA 兼容性。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 若某 Sponsor 在 Phase 3 IND 階段就要求 CDMO 建立 reprocessing 協議，這與 PACMP 的時機有何關係？
  2. CTD Module 3 中哪個小節最適合放置 reprocessing 協議？（提示：3.2.S 或 3.2.P）
4.2 Regulatory Guidance 法規指引（ICH 指引彙整）

原文內容 Original Text

See Table 4.2-1 below for a comprehensive overview of guidance on reprocessing/reworking across relevant ICH guidelines. Key ICH guidelines covered include ICH Q7 (GMP for APIs), ICH Q9(R1) (Quality Risk Management), and ICH Q13 (Continuous Manufacturing).

Under ICH Q7, the following principles apply:

  • Reprocessing of APIs: Repeating a crystallization step or other appropriate chemical or physical manipulation steps is generally considered acceptable. However, if such reprocessing is used for a majority of batches, it should be included as part of the standard manufacturing process.
  • Continuation after in-process control: Continuation of a process step after an in-process control test has shown that the step is incomplete is considered to be part of the normal process — NOT reprocessing.
  • Unreacted material: Introducing unreacted material back into a process and repeating a chemical reaction is considered reprocessing unless it is part of the established process. Such reprocessing should be preceded by careful evaluation to ensure product quality is not adversely impacted.

Under ICH Q7 Reworking:

  • Before a decision is taken to rework batches, an investigation into the reason for non-conformance should be performed.
  • Reworked batches should be subjected to appropriate evaluation, testing, stability testing if warranted, and documentation.
  • Concurrent validation is often the appropriate validation approach for rework procedures.
  • Procedures should provide for comparing the impurity profile of each reworked batch against batches manufactured by the established process.

Under ICH Q7 Q&A: It may be acceptable to reprocess or rework expired API where the API manufacturer has all related historical GMP documentation and additional stability data. There may be registration/filing considerations beyond the scope of ICH Q7.

Under ICH Q9(R1): Quality Risk Management applies to materials management — assessment and evaluation of suppliers and contract manufacturers, use of materials, and to determine appropriateness of reprocessing, reworking, use of returned goods.

Under ICH Q13 (Continuous Manufacturing): In the event of a filter failure, a clear strategy for material diversion and refiltration (reprocessing) should be defined. Filtration steps in CM may be subject to longer filtration periods — control strategy must allow for filter changes and pre/post-use integrity testing without interrupting the process.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

ICH Q7 的重要區分：「製程步驟尚未完成時繼續執行」≠ reprocessing。例如：過濾尚未達到目標流量，繼續過濾屬正常製程；但若過濾失敗後重新過濾（refiltration），則屬 reprocessing。此區分對無菌充填步驟的 CDMO 至關重要。

Concurrent Validation（同步驗證）：不等待三批完整驗證批次，而是在 reworking 批次生產同時執行驗證。適用於一次性或極少數批次的 rework 情境，但需要預先定義接受標準。

比喻說明 Analogy

ICH Q7 對 reprocessing vs. 正常製程的區分，就像餐廳廚師：
• 牛排還沒熟，繼續烤 → 正常製程（non-reprocessing）
• 牛排煎焦了，切除焦皮重新調味 → reworking
• 牛排快焦時取出冷卻後再烤 → reprocessing（若事先定義在 SOP 中則可接受）

重點提示 Key Notes

過期 API 的 reprocessing（ICH Q7 Q&A）：技術上可行，但必須同時滿足：(1) 完整 GMP 歷史紀錄、(2) 額外穩定性數據、(3) 確認是否需要補充申報。台灣 CDMO 若為 Sponsor 提供此類服務，務必在 QTA 中明確責任歸屬——申報義務仍在 MAH（上市許可持有人），不在 CMO。

ICH Q13 與連續製造：隨著 CM 技術導入生物製劑，過濾失敗後的 refiltration 策略需在 CPMP（Continuous Process Monitoring Plan）中預先定義，不可事後補救。

實務應用 Practical Application

台灣某 CDMO 在批量配製後的無菌過濾（sterile filtration）發生 integrity test 失敗。此情況下：
(1) 若 BLA 或 PACMP 中已有預先核准的 refiltration 協議 → 屬 reprocessing（approved protocol），申報層級較低（AR 或 CBE）
(2) 若無預先核准協議 → 屬 reprocessing without approved protocol → PAS 層級（需 FDA 批准後才能放行）
決策原則：Sterility（無菌保證）優先 → 不確定時必須向 Regulatory Authority 確認

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 依 ICH Q9(R1)，如何利用 Quality Risk Management 決定某批 reprocessing 的可接受性？
  2. 若 reprocessing 發生在「大多數批次」，ICH Q7 如何要求處理？為何這對 BLA 申報有重大影響？

Table 4.2-1 Regulatory Guidance on Reprocessing/Reworking — ICH Guidelines 法規指引彙整

ICH Guideline Topic Guidance on Reprocessing/Reworking
ICH Q7: Good Manufacturing Practice Guide for Active Pharmaceutical Ingredients Reprocessing Introducing an intermediate or API back into the process and reprocessing by repeating a crystallization step or other appropriate chemical or physical manipulation steps (e.g., distillation, filtration, chromatography, milling) that are part of the established manufacturing process is generally considered acceptable. However, if such reprocessing is used for a majority of batches, such reprocessing should be included as part of the standard manufacturing process.

Continuation of a process step after an in-process control test has shown that the step is incomplete is considered to be part of the normal process. This is not considered to be reprocessing.

Introducing unreacted material back into a process and repeating a chemical reaction is considered to be reprocessing unless it is part of the established process. Such reprocessing should be preceded by careful evaluation to ensure that the quality of the intermediate or API is not adversely impacted due to the potential formation of by-products and over-reacted materials.
Reworking Before a decision is taken to rework batches that do not conform to established standards or specifications, an investigation into the reason for non-conformance should be performed.

Batches that have been reworked should be subjected to appropriate evaluation, testing, stability testing if warranted, and documentation to show that the reworked product is of equivalent quality to that produced by the original process. Concurrent validation is often the appropriate validation approach for rework procedures.

Procedures should provide for comparing the impurity profile of each reworked batch against batches manufactured by the established process.
Q&A on Expired API It may be acceptable to reprocess or rework the expired API where the API manufacturer has all related historical GMP documentation and additional stability data on the reworked or reprocessed API. There may be registration/filing considerations that are beyond the scope of ICH Q7 in addition to the GMP considerations.
ICH Q9(R1): Quality Risk Management Materials Management Quality Risk Management as part of materials management — assessment and evaluation of suppliers and contract manufacturers; use of materials; to determine appropriateness of reprocessing, reworking, use of returned goods.
ICH Q13: Continuous Manufacturing of Drug Substances and Drug Products Filter Management in CM Filtration steps in CM may be subject to longer filtration periods and potentially increased throughput per unit area or a greater number of filter changes than those under batch manufacturing. A control strategy and a clearly defined scheme should be put in place to allow for filter changes and pre- and post-use integrity testing, as appropriate, without interrupting the process. In the event of a filter failure, a clear strategy for material diversion and refiltration (reprocessing) should be defined.

台灣 CDMO 解讀：ICH Q7 適用於 Drug Substance（API）製造；ICH Q9(R1) 提供風險決策框架；ICH Q13 針對連續製造中的過濾管理。生物製劑 Drug Product 的 sterile filtration 屬 ICH Q7 原則延伸應用。

4.3 Specific Guidance from the United States (FDA) 美國 FDA 特定指引

原文內容 Original Text

In addition to implementation of the ICH Guidelines, the FDA provides general guidance for biologicals during the clinical investigation period and specific guidance for biologicals during the post-market approval period.

4.3.1 During Clinical Investigation Period

In 2008, FDA published Guidance for Industry: CGMP for Phase 1 Investigational Drugs that stressed the importance of documenting how the manufacturing process was carried out during the clinical investigational period:

  • A record of manufacturing data that details the materials, equipment, procedures used, and any problems encountered during manufacturing. Manufacturers should retain records sufficient to replicate the manufacturing process.
  • A record of changes in procedures and processes used for subsequent batches along with the rationale for any changes.

Since reprocessing and/or reworking are significant changes, they are required to be reported to the FDA under an information amendment to the Investigational New Drug (IND) Application on file to carry out the human clinical trials (21 CFR 312.31). Although there is no required time period of delay of implementation for these information amendments, manufacturers typically wait for a period of time to allow the FDA reviewers opportunity to review the amendment.

Note: "Consider the impact of changes to be discussed with regulatory authorities in order to determine the need for additional toxicology studies."

FDA in 2020 published Guidance for Industry: CMC Information for Human Gene Therapy Investigational New Drug Applications (INDs). While there is no mention of reworking, the following guidance for reprocessing applies:

  • Drug Substance: For early stage INDs, there may be differences between manufacturing of toxicology lots and clinical study material. For later stage INDs, process changes or reprocessing step(s) may exist. Describe how manufacturing differences are expected to impact product safety and activity; provide batch analysis in CTD Section 3.2.S.4.4.
  • Drug Product: Under certain conditions, repeating sterile filtration (if applicable) may be critical. Clearly describe the conditions and justifications for each reprocessing procedure and demonstrate product consistency between reprocessed lots and normal production lots.

4.3.2 Post-Market Approval Period

Under 21 CFR 601.12, each post-approval change in the production process established in the approved BLA must be reported using the submission type associated with one of the three tier-based reporting categories. This depends on the potential (i.e., risk) of the change to have an adverse effect on the identity, strength, quality, purity, or potency of the product. The submission types are:

  • Prior Approval Supplement (PAS): Change that has a substantial potential to have an adverse effect on product quality (major changes). A PAS must be approved by FDA prior to distribution of the product manufactured using the change (21 CFR 601.12(b)).
  • Changes Being Effected in 30 Days / CBE (CBE-30/CBE): Changes that have a moderate potential to have an adverse effect on product quality. Report at least 30 days prior to distribution (21 CFR 601.12(c)).
  • Annual Report (AR): Changes that have a minimal potential to have an adverse effect. Documented by the applicant in an annual report (21 CFR 601.12(d)).

In 1997, FDA published Guidance for Industry: Changes to an Approved Application for Specified Biotechnology and Specified Synthetic Biological Products. Key provision: reprocessing without a previously approved reprocessing protocol is considered a change with substantial potential to adversely affect product quality, safety, or effectiveness — requiring a PAS.

In 2021, FDA published Guidance for Industry: Chemistry, Manufacturing, and Controls Changes to an Approved Application: Certain Biological Products (scope includes vaccines, plasma-derived protein products, cellular and gene therapy products). Table 4.3.2-1 lists the guidance provided for both reprocessing and reworking. See Table 4.3.2-1 below.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

IND Information Amendment（IND 資訊修正案）：在臨床試驗期間，若製造過程發生 reprocessing 或 reworking，需向 FDA 提交 21 CFR 312.31 資訊修正案。重點：無強制等待期，但業界慣例是等待 FDA 審閱機會再繼續。這不同於上市後 PAS 的強制等待。

21 CFR 601.12 三層申報架構：

  • PAS（Prior Approval Supplement）= 大幅變更，需等待 FDA 批准（通常 6–12 個月）
  • CBE-30 = 中度變更，提交後等待 30 天即可放行
  • AR（Annual Report）= 輕微變更，年度報告時一併揭露

重點提示 Key Notes

關鍵裁定：無預先核准協議 = PAS
依 1997 年 FDA 指引，reprocessing without a previously approved protocol 直接歸類為 PAS。這是實務上最常見的陷阱：CDMO 在緊急情況下執行 refiltration，若 BLA 未包含此協議，即觸發 PAS——批次必須扣留至 FDA 批准。
對策：PACMP 預先涵蓋所有預期 reprocessing 步驟。

實務應用 Practical Application — 台灣 CDMO 服務美國 Sponsor

場景：台灣 CDMO 執行 BLA 商業批生產，無菌過濾後 integrity test 失敗，執行 refiltration。

情境 FDA 申報類別 批次放行時機
BLA 含已核准 refiltration 協議 CBE 或 AR 30 天後或年度揭露
BLA 無協議，首次發生 PAS 等待 FDA 批准（≥6 個月）

決策優先順序：Sterility（無菌保證）→ CQA → Business。若過濾失敗批次無菌性存疑，廢棄優先於申請 PAS 放行。

比喻說明 Analogy

PAS / CBE-30 / AR 就像建築改建許可：
• PAS = 大型結構變更，需完整重新審查建照（等待核准才能動工）
• CBE-30 = 中型內部裝修，30 天後若無異議即可動工
• AR = 小型修繕，年底統一申報備案即可
CDMO 的工作就是在設計階段（PACMP）就把所有「可能要做的裝修」預先納入建照，避免緊急時面對 PAS 的漫長等待。

TFDA 對應說明

台灣 TFDA 法規對於製造場址位於台灣的 CDMO，主要參照 PIC/S GMP 規範（EMA 架構），但若 Sponsor 為美國廠商且申請 FDA BLA，則批次申報義務依 21 CFR 601.12 執行，由 MAH（BLA holder，通常為 Sponsor）承擔。CDMO 需在 QTA（品質技術協議）中明確規定：發生 reprocessing 時，CDMO 需在多少工作天內通知 Sponsor，以便 Sponsor 決定申報類別。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 為何 reworking（相對於 reprocessing）在 FDA 2021 年指引的 CBE-30 或 AR 欄位中顯示 "N/A"？這代表什麼含義？
  2. IND 期間 information amendment 的「無強制等待期」對 CDMO 的風險管理有何影響？

4.4 Specific Guidance from the European Union (EMA) 歐盟 EMA 特定指引

原文內容 Original Text

In addition to implementation of the ICH Guidelines, EMA provides specific guidance for biologicals both during the clinical investigation period and the post-market approval period.

4.4.1 During Clinical Investigation Period

EMA in 2022 published the Guideline on the Requirements for Quality Documentation Concerning Biological Investigational Medicinal Products in Clinical Trials – Revision 2. Scope included proteins and polypeptides (produced from recombinant and nonrecombinant cell-culture expression systems), their derivatives and products of which they are components (e.g., conjugates), and auxiliary medicinal products. There is no mention of reworking; however, the following guidance is provided for reprocessing:

  • Drug Substance: Any reprocessing during manufacture of the active substance (e.g. filter integrity test failure) should be described and justified. Reprocessing could be considered in exceptional circumstances. For biological products, these situations are usually restricted to certain refiltration and re-concentration steps upon technical failure of equipment or mechanical breakdown of a chromatography column.
  • Drug Product: Reprocessing may be acceptable for particular manufacturing steps (e.g. refiltration) only if the steps are adequately described and appropriately justified.

A change to the production process submitted in the investigational medicinal product dossier (IMPD), if it is a substantial modification, must be reported. Substantial modification means any change that is likely to have a substantial impact on the safety and rights of the subjects or on the reliability and robustness of the data generated in the clinical trial. See Table 4.4.1-1 below.

In 2025, EMA published the Guideline on Quality, Non-Clinical and Clinical Requirements for Investigational Advanced Therapy Medicinal Products in Clinical Trials (scope: gene therapy medicinal products, somatic cell therapy medicinal products, tissue-engineered products, combined ATMPs). No mention of reworking; guidance for reprocessing:

  • Drug Substance: Reprocessing could only be considered in exceptional circumstances. Usually restricted to refiltration and re-concentration steps upon technical failure.
  • Drug Product: Reprocessing may be acceptable for particular manufacturing steps (e.g. refiltration) only if adequately described and appropriately justified.

4.4.2 Post-Market Approval Period

Under the EMA Variation Regulation, each post-approval change in the production process established in the approved Marketing Authorisation Application (MAA) must be reported using the submission type associated with one of the three tier-based reporting categories. The submission types are:

  • Type II Major Variation: Change must be approved by EMA prior to distribution of the product manufactured using the change.
  • Type IB Minor Variation: Change must wait 30 days after submission to EMA.
  • Type IA Minor Variation: Change must be submitted within 12 months from the date of implementation.

There is no mention of reworking in the Variation Regulation. Table 4.4.2-1 provides guidance for reprocessing biological manufacturing processes. See Table 4.4.2-1 below.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

IMPD（Investigational Medicinal Product Dossier，試驗性醫療產品檔案）：等同於 FDA IND 的歐盟對應文件。臨床試驗期間，若製造過程發生 reprocessing，需評估是否構成 "substantial modification"；若是，需向成員國主管機關申報。

EMA Variation Regulation 三層分類：

  • Type II（重大變更）≈ FDA PAS
  • Type IB（次要變更）≈ FDA CBE-30
  • Type IA（微小變更）≈ FDA AR（但時間規定不同：12 個月內申報）

重點提示 Key Notes — EMA 對 Reworking 的態度

EMA 指引（2022 臨床期 + Variation Regulation 商業期）均完全不提及 reworking。這並非疏漏，而是 EMA 立場：生物製劑的 reworking 被視為不可接受或極端例外，預設要求 case-by-case 洽詢 EMA，無標準化申報路徑。

相較之下，FDA 2021 年指引雖也對 reworking 列出 N/A，但至少在表格中明確呈現，暗示需個案評估。EMA 連提都不提，代表其態度更為保守。

比喻說明 Analogy — EMA vs. FDA 文化差異

FDA 對 reprocessing/reworking 的態度較為「工程導向」：只要有充分數據支持，就可以找到一條申報路徑。EMA 較為「預防原則導向」：生物製劑的 reworking 幾乎等同於重新生產，preferably avoided。

台灣 CDMO 同時服務 FDA 和 EMA 市場時，應以 EMA 較嚴格的立場為設計基準——若能通過 EMA 的 "exceptional circumstances" 要求，FDA 端通常也可接受。反之則不然。

實務應用 Practical Application — FDA vs. EMA 申報對照

台灣 CDMO 同時為美國和歐洲市場生產同一生物製劑 Drug Product，發生 refiltration（有預先核准協議）：

市場 申報類別 放行時機 備註
FDA (BLA) AR 立即（年度報告揭露） 有核准協議，最寬鬆
EMA (MAA) Type IA 立即（12 個月內申報） 實施後申報，與 AR 類似
TFDA (Taiwan) 依 PIC/S 對應 參照 EMA Type IA/IB TFDA 依 PIC/S，偏 EMA 架構

TFDA 說明：台灣 TFDA 藥品 CMC 申報主要依 PIC/S Annex 1 及相關 EMA 指引，對 reprocessing 申報採 EMA 類比框架。若 CDMO 同時持有 Taiwan 藥品許可，應另行確認 TFDA 個案要求。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. EMA 2022 指引將 Drug Substance reprocessing 限定於 "exceptional circumstances"，而 FDA 允許以協議預先核准。這對 CDMO 的 reprocessing 開發策略有何影響？
  2. 若某批次在臨床期間（IMPD 已提交）需要 reprocessing，如何判斷是否構成 EMA 定義的 "substantial modification"？

Table 4.4.1-1 Guidance for Reporting Reprocessing of Biological Processes (EMA Clinical Period) EMA 臨床期 Reprocessing 申報指引

Substantial Modification 重大修正（需申報） Non-Substantial Modification 非重大修正（無需申報）
Manufacturing process of the active substance: any reprocessing not described in the IMPD
原料藥製造過程中：IMPD 未載明的任何 reprocessing		 Manufacturing process of the active substance: reprocessing if adequately described and accepted in the initial submission
原料藥製造過程中：已在初始提交中充分描述且獲接受的 reprocessing

解讀：IMPD 中有描述 = 非重大修正（免申報）；IMPD 中無描述 = 重大修正（需申報）。與 FDA 邏輯一致：事先在申請案中納入協議，可大幅降低事後申報負擔。
資料來源：EMA Guideline on Requirements for Quality Documentation — Biological IMPs in Clinical Trials, Revision 2 (2022)

比較鍵：B.I.a.2(c) 針對 Drug Substance；B.II.b.3(c) 針對 Drug Product（需 comparability assessment）。台灣 CDMO 若需執行 DS 或 DP reprocessing，應評估是否觸發 comparability study 要求。

4.5 Other Guidance 其他法規指引（WHO / PIC/S / BioPhorum / PDA）

原文內容 Original Text

Biological manufacturers wish to operate across many geographical areas, yet not all countries participate in ICH (e.g., Russia). Keeping track of each country's or region's CMC regulatory compliance review procedures and oversight for reprocessing and reworking of biologicals has proven challenging.

Various specialized government agencies and industry associations provide recommendations on effective control and safety when considering reprocessing and/or reworking of biological manufacturing processes:

  • World Health Organization (WHO): A United Nations agency to support health around the world, including the safety of manufactured drugs.
  • Pharmaceutical Inspection Co-Operation Scheme (PIC/S): An informal, nonbinding cooperative arrangement between regulatory authorities in the field of GMPs for medicinal products.
  • BioPhorum: A collaboration of industry leaders and subject matter experts working together to pool knowledge, best practices, and ideas on global biopharmaceutical industry practices.
  • Parenteral Drug Association (PDA): The leading global provider of science, technology, and regulatory information detailed in technical reports and points-to-consider documents.

Overall, carrying out reprocessing or reworking according to the principles indicated in the ICH guidelines and the FDA and EMA guidances is generally a safe approach. However, if there is any doubt about proceeding with reprocessing or reworking a biological manufacturing process, contact the respective regulatory authority for specific guidance.

Note: "If reprocessing or reworking has not been explicitly mentioned in the manufacturer's submitted documentation on the manufacturing process, correctly assume that it has not yet been approved."

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

PIC/S（Pharmaceutical Inspection Co-Operation Scheme）：目前有 57 個成員監管機構，包括 TFDA（台灣）、TGA（澳洲）、Health Canada 等。PIC/S GMP Guide 主要跟隨 EMA GMP 指引架構，並定期與 EMA Annex 同步更新。因此，TFDA GMP 要求本質上與 EMA 高度一致。

PIC/S 非法規機構，無法律約束力，但其成員機構彼此承認 GMP 查廠結論（Mutual Recognition），大幅降低重複稽查負擔。

重點提示 Key Notes — 黃金準則

本節結尾的 Note 是全章最重要的操作原則：

「若 reprocessing 或 reworking 未在已提交的製造過程文件中明確提及，應正確假設其尚未獲批准。」

這意味著：沉默 ≠ 允許。在不確定時，必須聯繫主管機關確認，而非逕行執行並事後報告。CDMO 在接受 Sponsor 授權前，應確認 BLA/MAA/IND 中是否已有明確的 reprocessing 條款。

實務應用 Practical Application — TFDA 與全球 Sponsor 的交集

台灣 CDMO 的監管三角：

  • TFDA（台灣藥品申請）→ PIC/S GMP，參照 EMA 架構
  • FDA（美國 Sponsor BLA）→ 21 CFR 601.12，三層申報制
  • EMA（歐洲 Sponsor MAA）→ Variation Regulation，Type II/IB/IA

實務建議： 1. QTA（品質技術協議）中應明確規定：哪些事件構成 reprocessing，CDMO 的通知義務時限（建議 3–5 工作天），以及由哪方承擔申報責任（通常為 MAH/Sponsor）。
2. CDMO 的 Site Master File（SMF）應包含 reprocessing 的一般框架政策，避免逐一 Sponsor 重複協商。
3. BioPhorum 發布的 reprocessing 最佳實務文件可作為 SOP 撰寫的技術參考。

比喻說明 Analogy

WHO / PIC/S / BioPhorum 就像國際外送平台（Uber Eats）的評分與規則：
• FDA = 美國市場的法律（強制性）
• EMA = 歐盟市場的法律（強制性）
• PIC/S = 國際 GMP 標準（準強制性，因為成員機構相互承認）
• WHO / BioPhorum = 業界最佳實踐建議（非強制，但具重要參考價值）
台灣 CDMO 同時在 FDA 和 EMA 這兩個「市場」服務客戶，必須同時遵守兩套法律，並以 PIC/S 標準確保自身 GMP 狀態。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. TFDA 基於 PIC/S 成員身份，在 reprocessing 申報上最接近 EMA 還是 FDA 的框架？為何此了解對台灣 CDMO 的 Sponsor 溝通至關重要？
  2. BioPhorum 和 PDA 的指引（非法規義務）在實務上何時應優先參考？
  3. 若某東南亞市場（非 ICH 成員）的 Sponsor 要求台灣 CDMO 執行 reworking，應如何建立申報策略？

Regulatory Comparison: FDA vs. EMA vs. PIC/S — Reprocessing/Reworking Reporting 法規三方比較：申報類別對照

情境 / Scenario FDA (BLA, 21 CFR 601.12) EMA (MAA, Variation Regulation) PIC/S / TFDA 實務建議 / Recommendation

決策優先順序（TR74 核心原則）：無菌保證（Sterility Assurance）→ 關鍵品質屬性（CQA）→ 商業考量（Business）。任何 reprocessing/reworking 決策均需遵守此優先順序；若無菌性存疑，廢棄批次優先於申請任何層級的申報。

本節重點回顧 Section Summary

  • ICH 協調框架：PACMP 是預先核准 reprocessing 的黃金工具，可將事後申報從 PAS 降至 AR/Type IA，是 CDMO 設計階段最重要的策略。
  • FDA 三層架構：無協議 = PAS（批次扣留至核准）；有協議 = AR；Reworking = N/A（個案洽詢）。關鍵依據：21 CFR 601.12 及 FDA 1997/2021 年指引。
  • EMA 三層架構：無協議重大 reprocessing = Type II（需核准）；有協議低風險 = Type IA（12 個月內申報）；Reworking 完全未提及（比 FDA 更保守）。
  • TFDA 定位：PIC/S 成員，主要跟隨 EMA 架構。台灣 CDMO 在 QTA 中應明確 reprocessing 通知義務時限與申報責任歸屬。
  • 黃金準則：「文件未提及 = 未核准」。在不確定時，聯繫主管機關優先於任何製造決策。
  • 決策優先順序：無菌保證 → CQA → Business。若無菌性存疑，廢棄優先於申報放行。
5

Section 5: Introduction to Reworking

返工概論 | p30-p54

Part A: 5.0–5.5 | PDA Technical Report No. 74 (Revised 2026) | p30–p44

本章學習目標

  • 掌握生物製劑 Reworking（返工）的法規定義、MAH 主責框架，及其與 Reprocessing（再加工）的本質區別 (TR74 §5.0, §5.2)
  • 能運用 MoSCoW 優先順序工具，以病患為中心評估返工活動的優先程度 (TR74 §5.1)
  • 理解製造變更的法規分類（FDA PAS / EMA Type II Variation），識別哪些變更構成返工觸發條件 (TR74 §5.3)
  • 熟悉主動返工協議（Proactive Reworking Agreement, PRA）的九步驟流程，及其在 CDMO 環境下的責任劃分 (TR74 §5.4)
  • 理解 ICH Q9(R1) 風險知識無限循環（RKI Cycle）如何指引返工決策中的知識管理與風險評估 (TR74 §5.5)
5.0 Introduction to Reworking 返工概論導言

原文內容 Original Text

It is the primary responsibility of the Manufacturing Authorization Holder (MAH) of a biological drug substance and/or drug product to consistently meet all quality, safety, purity, and identity requirements. This authoring team has strict recommendations on how and when such a reworking action should be considered by the MAH. The ultimate approval of a reworked drug substance and/or drug product for human use is solely at the discretion of the approving regulatory agency.

ICH and EU define reworking as:

"Subjecting an intermediate or API that does not conform to standards or specifications to one or more processing steps that are different from the established manufacturing process to obtain acceptable quality intermediate or API." (ICH Q7; EU GMP)

During reworking, the nonconforming material is subjected to a different manufacturing process to get a product that meets all the predefined acceptance criteria and specifications for quality, safety, purity, and identity (QSIP).

The scope of reworking for biologicals includes a diverse array of therapeutic proteins, each with unique challenges and considerations for manufacturing and quality control including, among others:

  • Interferons
  • Cytokines
  • Growth factors
  • Interleukins
  • Coagulation factors
  • Blood factors
  • Monoclonal antibodies (IgM, IgD, IgG, IgE, IgA)
  • Bispecific antibodies (IgG-based bsAbs, fragment-based bsAbs)
  • Antibody drug conjugates targeting cancer therapy
  • Fusion proteins
  • Glycoprotein hormones (e.g., rhCG, rFSH)
  • Insulins
  • Vaccines

Each of these therapeutic categories requires specific attention to factors like protein stability, aggregation prevention, and purification processes to ensure product purity, quality, efficacy, and safety.

Due to the intricate sourcing, including the nature of their manufacturing processes and stability concerns, cell and gene therapies are excluded from the scope for reworking. The complexity of these treatments often involves different considerations that require specialized processes and controls distinct from those applicable to the protein-based biologicals listed above.

Figure 5.0-1 gives an overview of possible areas of reworking for biological drug substances and drug products, applicable ICH guidances, and relevant PDA technical reports that enable documentation to write appropriate control strategies.

Figure 5.0-1
Overview of Reworking of Biological Drug Substances and Drug Products
[圖片佔位 — Fig 5.0-1: 包含 DS/DP 返工區域、相關 ICH 指引與 PDA TR 交叉引用的總覽圖]

Figure 5.0-1: Overview of Reworking of Biological Drug Substances and Drug Products (TR74 p31)

Referenced ICH guidelines include: ICH Q5A(R2), Q5C, Q5E, Q6B, Q7, Q9(R1), Q10, Q12. Referenced PDA Technical Reports include TR1, TR3, TR13, TR13-2, TR14, TR15, TR22, TR26, TR27, TR28, TR29, TR38, TR40, TR41, TR44, TR47, TR48, TR49, TR53, TR54, TR54-2, TR54-4, TR54-5, TR57, TR60, TR60-3, TR61, TR66, TR69, TR71, TR73, TR73-2, TR81, TR83, TR90, TR91.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

MAH（Marketing Authorization Holder，上市許可持有人）: 對藥品在整個生命週期中的品質、安全性及有效性負有最終法規責任的組織。在 CDMO 模型下，MAH 通常是委託方（Sponsor），而非 CMO 本身。

QSIP: Quality（品質）、Safety（安全性）、Purity（純度）、Identity（鑑別）—— 四位一體的藥品品質核心判斷軸。

Reworking（返工）核心定義: 將不符規格的中間體或 API，送入「與既定製程不同的」一個或多個步驟。這個「不同」是返工與再加工的分水嶺，詳見 5.2 節。

比喻說明 Analogy

想像一批精品威士忌桶在陳年過程中因溫控失誤，導致酒液品質不符標準。

  • 再加工（Reprocessing）= 重新裝回原型桶，按原始陳年程序重來一次 → 同樣的步驟、已知的結果。
  • 返工（Reworking）= 決定改用過桶技術（wine cask finish），用一個原始工藝計畫以外的新步驟來修正 → 不同的步驟、未知的風險 → 必須預先向監管機關申報核准。

對生物製劑而言，這瓶「威士忌」是活蛋白分子，容錯率遠低於烈酒，每一個額外步驟都可能影響免疫原性（immunogenicity）。

重點提示 Key Notes

細胞與基因治療（CGT）不在返工範圍內。TR74 明確將 CGT 排除，原因是其製程複雜性、活細胞/病毒載體的特殊性，以及返工操作本身可能對產品造成無法回復的改變。在 CDMO 如遇 CGT 批次 OOS，應直接棄批，不應嘗試返工。

決策框架: 無菌保證（Sterility）> 產品 CQA > 商業考量。返工永遠不能只因為批次成本而觸發——必須有明確的病患供應需求作為驅動力。

圖表解讀 Figure Analysis — Figure 5.0-1

此圖呈現生物製劑返工的全景地圖，分為三個維度：

  1. DS（原料藥）層面的返工區域：包含上游（細胞培養、發酵）與下游（純化、過濾、病毒清除）。
  2. DP（藥品製劑）層面的返工區域：配方、滅菌過濾、無菌充填、容器密封、凍乾等。
  3. 支撐文件網路：ICH 指引（Q5A、Q7、Q9、Q12 等）與 PDA TR（TR22、TR26、TR41 等）形成密集的交叉引用矩陣。

作為 CDMO，圖中最關鍵的應用點：了解哪個製程步驟出 OOS → 對應哪個適用指引 → 識別需要引用的 TR，才能正確起草 reworking protocol。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. ICH Q7 對 Reworking 的定義中，哪個關鍵詞決定了它與 Reprocessing 的本質差異？
  2. 為什麼細胞與基因治療被排除在 TR74 返工範圍之外？請從製程複雜性與病患安全兩個角度說明。
  3. 在一家無菌充填 CDMO 中，若 Sponsor 是 MAH，當一批 mAb 製劑出現 OOS 時，誰來做「要不要返工」的最終決定？CMO 的角色邊界在哪裡？
5.1 Prioritization Tool for Reworking 返工優先順序工具

原文內容 Original Text

Using the MoSCoW (Must-have, Should-have, Could-have, and Won't-have, or will not have right now) Prioritization Tool to evaluate reworking of a biological drug substance involves systematically categorizing tasks or issues based on their criticality and impact.

This step-by-step guide outlines how to apply the MoSCoW method in this context, and Figure 5.1-1 illustrates the Patient-Centric Reworking Prioritization tool.

1. Gather Relevant Data and Stakeholders

  • Collect all information related to the reworking process, including technical assessments, quality data, regulatory considerations, and risk analyses.
  • Assemble a cross-functional team comprising manufacturing, quality assurance, regulatory affairs, and process development experts.

2. Define the Scope of Reworking

  • Clearly specify which aspects of the biological drug substance are being considered for rework (e.g., purification, formulation, in-process controls, final product adjustments).

3. Identify Rework Tasks or Issues

  • List all potential rework activities, corrections, or modifications needed to meet quality and regulatory standards.

4. Apply the MoSCoW Prioritization Criteria
Categorize each task or issue into one of the following groups:

  • Must have (M): Critical for human survival, compliance, safety, efficacy, or regulatory approval. These are nonnegotiable and should be completed before proceeding.
  • Should have (S): Immediate medical supply need; can be scheduled after Must-Have items.
  • Could have (C): Desirable to support patient needs, especially those suffering with genetic disorders, cancer, glaucoma, blood issues, and wherever critical to support health condition of work force.
  • Won't have (W): Tasks that are not necessary in the current scope or can be deferred.

5. Prioritize Reworking Activities

  • Focus first on Must-Have tasks to ensure the reworked product meets all quality and regulatory standards.
  • Schedule Should-Have activities shortly afterwards, resources permitting.
  • Consider Could-Have tasks, if time and resources allow, to enhance overall process robustness.
  • Leave Won't-Have tasks for future considerations or continuous improvement.

6. Document and Communicate

  • Record the prioritization outcomes clearly, including rationales for each category.
  • Communicate the priorities to all relevant teams and stakeholders to ensure aligned execution.

7. Implement and Monitor

  • Proceed with rework activities according to the established priorities.
  • Monitor progress and adjust priorities if new information or issues arise.

8. Additional Measures

  • Ensure compliance with GMP and regulatory requirements throughout the rework process.
  • Use risk assessments to support the categorization, especially for CQAs.
Figure 5.1-1
Must-have, Should-have, Could-have, and Won't-have as a Patient-Centric Prioritization Tool
[圖片佔位 — Fig 5.1-1: MoSCoW 四象限與病患中心返工優先矩陣]

Figure 5.1-1: MoSCoW Patient-Centric Prioritization Tool (TR74 p34)

Systematically applying the MoSCoW prioritization method can effectively focus resources on the most-critical rework activities, ensuring the drug substance and/or drug product meets quality, safety, and regulatory standards efficiently.

"Importantly, the prioritization tool mentioned in this technical report serves as an example. The manufacturing organization must align with the company's quality system and utilize approved prioritization tools."

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

MoSCoW 法最初源自敏捷軟體開發，TR74 將其引入 GMP 返工決策框架，強調以病患為核心的優先排序，而非以商業壓力或成本回收為導向。

四個等級的 GMP 含義：

  • Must-have: 攸關病患存活、法規合規、產品安全有效性 → 不做等同無法放行
  • Should-have: 關鍵供應需求，但稍有時間餘裕 → 必須做，但可在 M 之後安排
  • Could-have: 強化製程韌性，支援特定病患群（罕見病、癌症）
  • Won't-have: 本次範圍外 → 納入 CAPA 或 CI（持續改善）計畫

比喻說明 Analogy

想像一座城市發生地震後的緊急應變指揮中心，如何分派搶救隊伍：

  • M：醫院、托嬰中心（有人命 → 立即動員所有資源）
  • S：幹道橋樑（影響整體救援，盡快修復）
  • C：公園圍牆（改善生活品質，資源允許時處理）
  • W：商業廣告招牌（本次不列優先）

返工亦然 — 在資源有限的 CDMO 環境，MoSCoW 幫助 QA 與管理層對齊同一語言，避免「商業壓力」偷偷把 W 級別的項目晉升為 M。

重點提示 Key Notes

TR74 強調：MoSCoW 只是示例工具，組織必須使用自身 QMS 中已核准的優先順序工具。這意味著若工廠 SOP 已有類似的批次棄留決策矩陣（例如基於 FMEA 或 RPN 的優先框架），可以整合取代，但核心病患中心原則不變。

CDMO 關鍵點：在臨床期 CDMO，每一批臨床試驗用藥（IMP）背後都有等待用藥的病患。MoSCoW 的 M 等級不是「我們想不想救這批藥」，而是「病患在等待這批藥嗎、而且替代品目前不存在嗎？」

圖表解讀 Figure Analysis — Figure 5.1-1

MoSCoW 四象限優先矩陣視覺化應包含以下要素：

  • 以同心圓或四象限呈現四個 MoSCoW 等級，由內（M）到外（W）代表緊迫度遞減
  • 病患圖示置於中心，強化「以病患為核心」的評估起點
  • 各象限列出對應的生物製劑特定考量點（如 M 區：CQA 衝擊、法規合規；S 區：供應鏈缺口；C 區：製程優化）

閱讀此圖時，應先問：「這個返工決策是從內圈（病患安全）向外擴展，還是被外圈（商業考量）向內擠壓？」任何由商業壓力驅動的返工評估，都是 GMP 合規的危險訊號。

實務應用 Practical Application

CDMO 場景：某臨床 II 期 mAb 批次純化後，蛋白質聚合體（aggregates）超標（CQA 不符）。Sponsor 要求緊急評估是否可以返工以維持臨床試驗時程。

請用 MoSCoW 框架評估以下項目：

  • M: 確認聚合體的免疫原性風險評估、確定病毒安全性不受返工影響
  • S: 評估額外 SEC-HPLC 監測計畫、起草返工協議草案
  • C: 小規模（bench scale）確認研究設計
  • W: 本次不考慮更換純化樹脂（屬於製程改善，非緊急返工範疇）

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 若同一批藥同時出現兩個問題：①聚合體超標（影響 CQA）、②標籤印刷錯誤（GDocP 問題），用 MoSCoW 如何排序？理由為何？
  2. TR74 說 MoSCoW 只是「示例工具」。若貴公司 QMS 中沒有類似工具，這句話對你意味著什麼行動？
5.2 Difference Between Reprocessing and Reworking 再加工與返工的區別

原文內容 Original Text

Table 5.2-1 and Table 5.2-2 outline the major differences between reprocessing (see Section 3.0) and reworking (see Section 5.0).

See full comparison tables below (Table 5.2-1 and Table 5.2-2).

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

這是 TR74 最核心的一組定義對比。掌握這兩個表格，等於掌握了 90% 的 GMP 返工法規邏輯。

最簡記憶法：

  • Reprocessing（再加工）= 原有製程中的重複步驟 → 法規提前授權可能已涵蓋
  • Reworking（返工）= 原有製程以外的新步驟 → 必須先提交法規申報、取得核准，才能執行

比喻說明 Analogy

把製造流程比喻成廚師的標準食譜（SOP）：

  • Reprocessing：湯太淡，把整鍋湯再熬一次（食譜裡本來就有這步驟，只是重做）
  • Reworking：湯太濃，加入食譜裡沒有的食材去中和（新步驟 → 食譜已變更 → 需要主廚（監管機關）簽字確認）

重點提示 Key Notes — Drug Product 的特殊性

Table 5.2-2 點出一個常被忽略的重要規則：

DP（藥品製劑）通常無法被「返工」，只能被「再加工」。

例如無菌充填過程中因機械故障而中斷，允許重新滅菌過濾後再充填（reprocessing），但無法在已充填的藥品上疊加一個「原始製程外的新步驟」——那等同於改變藥品本身。

對於無菌充填 CDMO 而言，DP 層級的 OOS 絕大多數情況下的結論是棄批，而非返工。

關鍵對比速記

Reprocessing → 重複既有步驟 → 可預先授權於 License
Reworking    → 引入新步驟   → 必須事先送審取得 PAS / Type II

Reprocessing → 包含機械故障導致的不合格
Reworking    → 僅限非機械故障的品質不合格批次

Reprocessing → 若大多數批次都用到，應納入標準製程
Reworking    → 每次事件唯一，不應常態化

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 某批 DS（原料藥）因離心機故障導致蛋白質回收率偏低，是否可以進行「返工（Reworking）」？為什麼？
  2. 一批 DP 無菌充填後發現有一個注射瓶容量不足（under-fill），這是否為 Reworking 的適用情境？
  3. 若一家 CDMO 每 5 批中有 3 批需要 Reprocessing，TR74 §5.2 對此有何明確指引？

Table 5.2-1: Reprocessing versus Reworking (TR74 §5.2, Ref. 40)

Reprocessing 再加工 Reworking 返工
Reprocessing is an exact repetition of one or more steps in the established manufacturing process Reworking is based on the inclusion of new steps in the established manufacturing process
To support annual product quality review, GMP requirements need to be followed within the QMS to support regulatory approval To support annual product quality review, GMP requirements need to be followed within the QMS to support regulatory approval
May be approved as part of the manufacturing license, or regulatory approval may be a post-approval supplement (see Section 3.0) Regulatory submission and formal approval are mandatory
Nonconforming batches (including mechanical equipment failures) Only nonconforming batches (does not include mechanical equipment failures)
Applicable to low-bioburden drug substance and sterile drug substance and/or drug product* (23, 41, 42) Applicable to low-bioburden drug substance and sterile drug substance and/or drug product* (23, 43–46)
Batch subjected to one or more steps that are part of established manufacturing process Batch subjected to one or more steps that are different from established manufacturing process
Contamination control strategy must be considered* (23, 41, 44, 47) Contamination control strategy must be considered* (23, 41, 44–47)
If reprocessing is used for a majority of batches, it should be included as part of the standard manufacturing process Each reworking event is unique and should not be part of the standard manufacturing process
Reprocessed batches should be subjected to appropriate evaluation Reworked batches should be subjected to appropriate evaluation, testing, and stability testing, if warranted, with documentation to demonstrate that the reworked batches are of equivalent quality to that produced by the original process* (2, 48)
Concurrent validation is often appropriate Concurrent validation is often appropriate

*For more information, refer to the references cited.

Table 5.2-2: Reprocessing and Reworking for Drug Substance and Drug Product (TR74 §5.2, Ref. 40)

Biological Intermediate / Drug Substance (API)
生物製劑中間體 / 原料藥		 Drug (Medicinal) Product
藥品製劑
Clear distinction between reprocessing and reworking Often, there is no clear distinction between reprocessing and reworking
Note: Drug products cannot be reworked, they must be reprocessed (e.g., sterile filtration in case of mechanical failures)
Reprocessing is typical Reprocessing is atypical
Reprocessing generally improves API quality
Note: In certain cases, reprocessing may restore or maintain API quality; however, it should not be considered a routine practice and must be scientifically justified on a case-by-case basis.		 Reprocessing rarely or possibly does not improve drug product quality except sterility attributes
Note: A detailed risk assessment is needed at this stage.
5.3 Background to Manufacturing Changes 製造變更背景說明

原文內容 Original Text

Reworking is an unexpected occurrence and is not preapproved as part of the marketing authorization. The MAH's Quality Unit should oversee investigations into a nonconforming (OOS) in-process drug, a bulk process intermediate (final biological bulk intermediate), a drug substance of a single batch or lot to an alternate manufacturing process during reworking decisions, prior to release to ensure that the details of rework in question has been submitted to the regulatory agency and formal approval has been obtained.

Changes that have a substantial potential to have an adverse effect on product quality (i.e., major variations) require the manufacturer (applicant) to report the change to the FDA in a supplement to the approved BLA. A PAS (Prior Approval Supplement) must be approved by the FDA prior to distribution of the product manufactured using the change to protect the public from products whose identity, strength, quality, purity, potency, safety, or effectiveness may be compromised (10, 33, 46).

If biological drug products are reworked, they must be reported in a supplement to FDA prior to distribution, unless the reworking was done according to a procedure previously approved by the Agency. The type of notification is based on the potential risk of the change having an adverse effect on the identity, strength, quality, purity, or potency of the product as it may relate to the safety or effectiveness of the product (24).

The Variation Regulation is supplemented by the European Commission's Guidelines on the Details of the Various Categories of Variations, on the Operation of the Procedures Laid Down in Chapters II, IIa, III and IV of Commission Regulation No 1234/2008 of 24 November 2008. The EU guidelines define a major variation of Type II as one that is not an extension of the Marketing Authorization and that may have a significant impact on the quality, safety, or efficacy of a medicinal product (37).

Figure 5.3-1 shows scientific and risk-based categorization changes and Table 5.3-1 provides major changes in manufacturing that can be designated as reworking.

Figure 5.3-1
Scientific and Risk-Based Approach to Categorization of Changes
[圖片佔位 — Fig 5.3-1: 基於科學與風險的變更分類決策樹 (Ref. 49)]

Figure 5.3-1: Scientific and Risk-Based Approach to Categorization of Changes (TR74 p37, Ref. 49)

See Table 5.3-1 below for major changes in manufacturing that can be designated as reworking.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

PAS（Prior Approval Supplement，事前核准補件）: FDA BLA 框架下，對已核准生物製劑的重大製程變更，必須提交 PAS 並取得 FDA 核准後，方可使用變更後製程生產並銷售產品。這是美國法規的「事前核准」機制。

Type II Variation（EMA）: 歐盟對上市許可的重大變更類別，定義為「對品質、安全性或有效性可能有顯著影響」的變更。等同於 FDA PAS 的歐盟版本。

BLA（Biologics License Application）: 美國生物製劑的上市許可申請書，相當於 NDA 之於化學藥品。

圖表解讀 Figure Analysis — Figure 5.3-1

此圖呈現製造變更的科學與風險導向分類決策路徑（Ref. 49），核心邏輯為：

  1. 定義變更範疇：該變更是否影響已建立條件（Established Conditions, EC）？是否影響 CQA 或 CPP？
  2. 風險評估：對病患安全、產品品質、有效性的潛在衝擊有多大？
  3. 法規分類：
    • 高風險 → PAS（FDA）/ Type II（EMA）→ 事前核准
    • 中風險 → CBE-30（FDA）/ Type IB（EMA）→ 事前通知
    • 低風險 → Annual Report（FDA）/ Type IA（EMA）→ 年度報告

返工（Reworking）因其引入「製程外新步驟」，原則上屬於高風險類別，幾乎必然落入 PAS / Type II 的管轄。

比喻說明 Analogy

想像製造授權（Marketing Authorization）是一份「政府核准的食品加工許可證」，上面列明允許使用的原料、加工步驟、設備規格。

  • 若你臨時換了一個「許可證上沒有列」的新加工步驟（返工）→ 等同於在食品工廠用了政府未審核的新加工程序 → 必須先重新申請許可（PAS / Type II），取得核准後才能出貨。
  • 出貨後才申報 = 違規 = 在台灣 TFDA 管轄下可能面臨批次召回。

重點提示 Key Notes — CDMO 責任邊界

誰提交 PAS / Type II Variation？

是 MAH（通常是 Sponsor），不是 CDMO。CDMO 的角色是：

  1. 發現不合格 → 立即通知 Sponsor QU
  2. 提供技術數據與評估支援
  3. 起草 reworking protocol（由 Sponsor QU 審核）
  4. 在取得監管核准後執行返工
  5. 不能在 Sponsor 未授權的情況下自行啟動或執行返工

若 CDMO 自行啟動返工而未取得 Sponsor 或監管機關核准，法規後果由 MAH（Sponsor）承擔，但商業合約的違約責任則指向 CDMO。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. FDA PAS 與 EMA Type II Variation 在觸發條件上是否完全一致？若不一致，CDMO 服務全球客戶時應如何處理？
  2. 若一個返工事件既涉及 DS（原料藥）也涉及 DP（製劑），法規申報策略上應一起提交還是分別提交？

Table 5.3-1: Changes in Manufacturing That Can Be Designated as Reworking (TR74 §5.3, Ref. 34, 50)

Position 部位 Major Changes 重大變更類型 Approach 處理方針
Downstream Processing
下游製程		 Changes in viral filtration step 病毒過濾步驟變更 Reworking should be science- and risk-based, considering such elements as the control strategy, comparability, ongoing process validation, and alignment with regulatory approval procedures prior to release of the drug substance or drug product.

返工應以科學與風險為基礎，考量管控策略、可比性、持續製程驗證，並在放行前確認已符合法規核准程序。

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

Proactive Reworking Agreement（PRA，主動返工協議）: 在啟動返工操作之前，MAH 主動與監管機關協商、提交詳細的返工協議（PACMP），取得預先核准，再執行返工的整體流程。

PACMP（Post-Approval Change Management Protocol）: ICH Q12 框架下的變更管理協議，預先定義變更範疇、研究計畫、接受標準，讓監管機關在執行前即審核確認。

PAS（Prior Approval Supplement）: FDA 對 BLA 重大補件的核准機制，監管機關核准前不得使用更改後的製程出貨。

圖表解讀 Figure Analysis — Figure 5.4-1

主動返工協議（PRA）流程圖呈現九個步驟的線性決策路徑，關鍵閘口（Gate）包含：

  • Step 1-2 閘口：QU 調查根因 → 決定棄批或啟動返工評估
  • Step 3-4 閘口：QU 詳細評估 → 起草 reworking protocol（PACMP 格式）
  • Step 5 閘口：正式送審（PAS/Type II）→ 等待監管核准（此步驟前不得執行任何返工操作）
  • Step 6 閘口：監管機關審查問答 → MAH 回覆 → 取得預先核准
  • Step 7-9 閘口：執行 → 評估 → 最終送審放行

整個 PRA 流程的核心精神：先問，後做。在 GMP 世界中，「先做後報」對返工而言是不被接受的。

比喻說明 Analogy

PRA 就像外科手術前的術前討論與家屬同意書流程：

  • 醫師（MAH/CMO）不能因為病患情況緊急，就跳過術前評估直接開刀
  • 必須先向病患家屬（監管機關）說明為什麼要手術、如何操作、預期結果是什麼
  • 取得知情同意（核准）後，才能進行手術（執行返工）
  • 手術後仍需完整記錄手術報告（最終送審）

重點提示 Key Notes — CDMO 的執行痛點

PRA 流程中最容易出問題的環節在 Step 1-3 之間：

生物分子在 OOS 發現後的「調查等待期」，若保存條件未達最優（非驗證保存時間、溫度偏差），蛋白質結構可能已發生不可逆變化。TR74 明確指出：若 QU 判斷「在調查等待期間蛋白質完整性已受損」，整個返工申請可能直接被 QU 否決（步驟 3 的 Note）。

實務結論：CDMO 的 GMP 日常管理重點之一，是確保 OOS 調查期間的保存條件記錄完整、可追溯，這是返工可行性的前提條件。

實務應用 Practical Application

CDMO 場景：週五下午 4 點，一批臨床 III 期 mAb 純化後發現宿主細胞蛋白（HCP）超標。QC 確認測試無誤，QU 啟動調查。此時應按 PRA 流程做什麼？

  1. 立即隔離批次，確認保存條件符合 DS 驗證儲存規範（不可超出 hold time）
  2. 通知 Sponsor QU（MAH），同步啟動聯合調查
  3. 確認根因：是層析樹脂性能下降？緩衝液配制錯誤？還是分析方法問題？
  4. 若根因確認後評估可能通過額外純化步驟降低 HCP → 啟動 PRA Step 3（詳細評估）
  5. 在獲得 Sponsor 授權且完成 PAS 提交並取得 FDA 核准前，禁止執行任何返工操作

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. PRA Step 3 的「Note」提到，長期保存在 OOS 狀態下的生物分子，QU 可能直接拒絕返工。這對 CDMO 的 OOS 調查 SOP 有什麼設計啟示？
  2. 若一個批次的 OOS 調查橫跨 6 週，分別由哪些角色（MAH QU / CDMO QA / Regulatory Affairs）承擔 PRA 流程中的哪些責任？

Table 5.4-1: Steps for the Proactive Reworking Agreement (PRA) (TR74 §5.4)

Steps 步驟 Information 說明
Step 1 Detection of any in-process nonconformance of a biological intermediate or nonconformance of a drug substance and/or drug product (refer Table 5.3-1 for changes associated with drug product) should be immediately brought to the attention of the Quality Unit and should be escalated to the appropriate level of management (i.e., site quality head).

Note: The failure of analytical methods or failure to meet any acceptance criteria is considered as nonconformance.

A detailed investigation or root cause analysis must be performed to understand in depth the exact reason of the nonconformance or failure to meet the acceptance criteria. Before this investigation starts, the analytical tests must be duplicated to confirm the nonconformance.

中文要點：發現不合格 → 立即上報 QU → 複驗確認 → 根因調查。
Step 2 Based on the stage of manufacturing, details, and the extent of nonconformance, after a detailed evaluation, the Quality Unit, cross-functional experts, and management may consider rejecting the nonconforming material/batch/lot or propose a "reworking strategy."

中文要點：QU + 跨職能專家評估 → 棄批 or 啟動返工策略。
Step 3 The Quality Unit will recommend carrying out a detailed assessment before granting permission to rework the drug substance or drug product that failed to meet specification based on the following preconditions detailed in Step 4. The assessment should be based on the application of science, knowledge, and risk approach.

Note: The structural stability of the biological molecule can be compromised if exposed to a longer period in non-validated hold time or conditions. Hence, often the reworking strategy of a drug substance that fails to meet the acceptance criteria can be "rejected" by the Quality Unit. This is due to the impact of the unusually long hold-period conditions of the biological molecule in a nonconformed state during the preliminary investigation steps (between Step 1 and Step 3).

A detailed review will be performed by the Quality Unit on conclusions of the science, knowledge, and risk assessment and can consider approving a "reworking procedure." The details from the assessment will be captured in the change control as stimulus for reworking.

中文要點：科學/知識/風險三軸評估 → QU 審核 → 若保存期超出驗證範圍，整案可能被 QU 直接否決。
Step 4 An adequate science/risk/knowledge-based strategy must be considered during the drafting of a detailed reworking protocol and its part of a change control activity. All the associated operating procedures, sampling plans, test procedures, and controls should be approved before entering into the draft protocol.

All considerations on stages, in-process control tests, enhanced sampling, acceptance criteria, batch/lot numbering, and proposal to store the reworked material under predefined conditions with a detailed strategy on validation (including strategy on small-scale studies) must be included as a part of the "reworking protocol" (PACMP). All the process changes, in-process controls, and additional testing methods should be thoroughly documented in the reworking protocol. The entire reworking protocol and test methods should be reviewed, commented on, and approved by the Quality Unit.

中文要點：起草 PACMP 格式的返工協議 → 含採樣計畫、接受標準、小規模研究策略 → QU 審核批准。
Step 5 Prior Submission Process: The Quality Unit formally approves a change as a part of the reworking protocol, submits the relevant document containing a detailed description on the reason for the change along with justifications, risk assessments, proposed studies, including acceptance criteria, supporting data to be generated during execution of reworking, validation strategy along with a detailed implementation plan within PACMPs on the reported category to the regulatory authority as PAS (FDA) and/or Type II Variation (EMA) (52). This set of detailed documents must be reviewed and approved by the regulators prior to the execution of the "reworking strategy."

中文要點：正式送審 PAS（FDA）/ Type II（EMA）→ 監管機關核准前，絕對不能執行返工。
Step 6 The regulatory agency reviews the "reworking protocol" (PACMP) plan of change and, including the studies proposed, can request additional details and can ask relevant questions on the change from the MAH during this phase of the Proactive Reworking Agreement (PRA). The MAH provides all the necessary details and answers and agrees to the execution of the preapproved reworking protocol.

Note: An applicant may ask FDA to expedite its review of a supplement for public health reasons or if a delay in making the change described in it would impose an extraordinary hardship on the applicant. Such a supplement should be plainly marked: "Prior Approval Supplement-Expedited Review Requested."

中文要點：監管機關問答階段 → MAH 回覆 → 緊急公衛需求可申請加速審查。
Step 7 The reworking protocol should be executed under strict supervision of manufacturing experts and Quality Assurance.

The in-process and control samples must be evaluated by Quality Control on a timely basis. The use of PAT (Process Analytical Technology) tools and documenting the real-time data gives a better overview about the performance of the biological molecule under the reworking conditions (54). Quality Control should additionally test to ascertain the quality and purity of the reworked material.

中文要點：在製造與 QA 嚴格監督下執行 → 建議使用 PAT 即時監測 → QC 充分測試返工物料。
Step 8 A detailed evaluation must be carried on reworked batches to ensure that product quality has not been compromised including, if necessary, using additional analytical test methods and stability testing (55, 56). Reworking materials and process documents should be reviewed and approved by the Quality Unit, and the impact on validation and stability should be evaluated.

Upon a detailed evaluation, the Quality Unit will take a position to proceed with a regulatory submission. The Regulatory Department will make necessary changes and additions in the regulatory documentation and, upon review, will inform to the regulatory authority and submit it as a PAS (FDA) and/or Type II Variation (EMA) (52).

中文要點：返工批次詳細評估含穩定性測試 → QU 決定是否進行法規最終送審。
Step 9 After submission of the detailed information and data to the regulatory agency in the prescribed format of reworking protocol, the agency will consider the specific time to review, comment, and ask for further data, if necessary, or approve the reworking for the proposed drug substance and/or drug product.

中文要點：監管機關最終審查 → 批准或要求補充資料 → 完成整個 PRA 循環。
5.5 Application of Knowledge and Risk Assessments 知識與風險評估的應用

原文內容 Original Text

ICH Quality Guideline Q10: Pharmaceutical Quality System was the first official global guideline known to firmly position QRM (Quality Risk Management) and knowledge management (KM) as important enablers of an effective pharmaceutical quality system (PQS). Specifically, QRM and KM jointly enable (i) achieving product realization, (ii) establishing and maintaining a state of control, (iii) facilitating continual improvement, and (iv) critical decision-making during the reworking strategy (57).

ICH Q9(R1) emphasizes the relationship between risk and knowledge, and it highlights the importance of KM in managing risks. It places knowledge and KM repeatedly and explicitly at the core of all QRM activities, further reinforcing the connection of scientific knowledge and risk in several other regulatory guidance documents. Specifically, the definition of risk-based decision-making reads:

"An approach to, or a process of, making decisions that considers knowledge about risks relevant to the decision and whether risks are at an acceptable level." (ICH Q9(R1))

The Risk Knowledge Infinity Cycle (RKI Cycle) establishes and promotes the following concepts:

  • Knowledge is both an input to and an output from QRM
  • Knowledge has an inverse relationship with risk
  • Knowledge should flow effortlessly and on demand to inform risk and risk-based decisions
  • The Cycle is continuous and perpetual

The RKI Cycle can be applied to support the goals of the PQS as defined in ICH Q10. A set of six principles corresponding with six "nodes" along the Cycle has been developed to better guide the tangible connection between QRM and KM practices as illustrated in Figure 5.5-1 (58).

Figure 5.5-1
Six Guiding Principles of the Risk Knowledge Infinity Cycle Framework
[圖片佔位 — Fig 5.5-1: RKI Cycle 六節點無限循環框架圖]

Figure 5.5-1: Six Guiding Principles of the Risk Knowledge Infinity Cycle Framework (TR74 p42, Ref. 58)

During the reworking of biologicals, rigorous risk management ensures that any changes or corrective actions do not compromise critical quality attributes, safety, or regulatory compliance. Structured assessments (e.g., FMEA within a quality risk management framework) prioritize controls and justify decisions, while robust change control, deviation tracking, and CAPA link risks to measurable outcomes. Effective knowledge management captures batch histories, tacit operator knowhow, prior rework learnings, and real-time analytics in a shared repository. This enables cross-functional review and consistent, evidence-based decisions that reduce variability and prevent repeat issues.

Knowledge
Prior knowledge is a critical tool to identify and justify quality during the critical planning, decision-making, and execution of the OOS of the biological drug substance or a drug product to be reworked. Three forms of knowledge are critical:

  1. Internal knowledge of the manufacturer gained throughout the product lifecycle (including development and characterization of biological drug substance and drug product) is the basis for identifying the elements of CMC that are established conditions (EC) (52), and those elements which are supportive information, historical development of products and/or similar processes, proprietary technologies, modelling data, previous regulatory filings, regulatory inspections, pre-approval manufacturing changes, compatibility assessments, CQAs and any signals associated with QSIP (4).
  2. External knowledge comes from public databases, literature surveys, journals, conferences, peer-reviewed publications and monographs.
  3. Knowledge application of scientific principles from biophysical sciences, pharmaceutical sciences, biochemical engineering, material science, and application of principles of engineering for evaluation of the structure-activity relationship of the molecule under investigation.

ICH Q9(R1) defines two primary principles of QRM:

  1. The evaluation of the risk to quality should be based on scientific knowledge and ultimately linked to the protection of the patient.
  2. The level of effort, formality, and documentation of the QRM process should be commensurate with the level of risk.

The details, in-depth information, and prior knowledge are critical during Step 2 of Table 5.4-1 and Figure 5.4-1 (PAR). Figure 5.5-1 provides an overview of the supporting information required to carry out a detailed assessment.

Figure 5.5-1 (Step 2 variant)
Information Required for Step 2 (Detailed Assessment)
[圖片佔位 — Fig 5.5-1 (Step 2): Step 2 詳細評估所需資訊的輸入/輸出架構圖（p44）]

Figure 5.5-1 (Step 2): Information Required for Step 2 — Detailed Assessment (TR74 p44)

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

RKI Cycle（Risk Knowledge Infinity Cycle，風險知識無限循環）: ICH Q9(R1) 所呼應的核心框架。以「無窮符號（∞）」形象呈現知識與風險的持續互動：知識越多 → 風險評估越精確 → 決策品質越高 → 產生更多知識，形成正向循環。

知識的三種形式（TR74 §5.5）：

  • 內部知識（Internal）: 製造商整個產品生命週期中積累的 CMC 數據、歷史批次資料、法規文件
  • 外部知識（External）: 文獻、期刊、研討會、公共數據庫
  • 知識應用（Application）: 將生物物理、藥學、生化工程等科學原理整合應用於特定分子的結構-活性關係分析

圖表解讀 Figure Analysis — Figure 5.5-1 (RKI Cycle)

RKI Cycle 六節點框架圖的核心結構：

  1. Knowledge Acquisition（知識獲取）: 彙整批次歷史、開發數據、外部文獻
  2. Knowledge Management（知識管理）: 結構化儲存、跨功能共享
  3. Risk Identification（風險識別）: 基於現有知識辨識潛在失效模式
  4. Risk Assessment（風險評估）: FMEA、FMECA、HACCP 等工具量化風險
  5. Risk Control（風險管控）: 設計管控措施並實施
  6. Risk Review（風險回顧）: 執行後反饋 → 更新知識庫 → 進入下一輪循環

在返工情境中，此循環的速度直接決定返工協議的科學說服力：知識越充足，QU 和監管機關越容易批准返工申請。

比喻說明 Analogy

RKI Cycle 就像一個有機農場的永續耕作循環：

  • 土壤分析（知識獲取）→ 選種施肥（知識應用）→ 病蟲害風險識別 → 有機防治策略（風險管控）→ 收成後土壤回復評估（風險回顧）→ 下一季種植（知識更新）
  • 「知識」就是土壤肥力——越豐富，下一季的「風險」越低，「決策品質」越高。

若一個 CDMO 對某 mAb 已積累了 20 批的 CMC 知識庫，其返工協議的科學說服力將遠大於只有 3 批歷史的廠商。

重點提示 Key Notes — ICH Q9(R1) 兩大 QRM 原則在返工中的應用

原則一：以科學知識為基礎，最終保護病患。
在返工中，這意味著每一個「允許返工」的決定，都必須有科學數據支撐（ICH Q9(R1) §3.1）：分析數據、穩定性數據、免疫原性評估，而不能只是「我們覺得應該沒問題」。

原則二：QRM 的投入程度與風險等級相稱。
這給了 CDMO 一個靈活空間：若根因很清楚、風險評估顯示影響極低，可以用較簡化的 QRM 工具（如 What-If）；若不確定性高，則必須用 FMEA 全套方法論（ICH Q9(R1) §3.2）。

知識與風險的反比關係

知識（K）↑  →  不確定性（U）↓  →  風險（R）↓

返工決策品質 ∝ 知識深度 × 知識廣度
             ∝ (內部知識 + 外部知識 + 知識應用)

RKI 循環：
知識 → QRM（識別/評估/管控）→ 決策 → 執行 → 反饋 → 更新知識
  ↑__________________________________|

實務應用 Practical Application

CDMO 場景：一個新承接的客戶 mAb 批次出現 OOS，但該產品在貴公司只有 2 批歷史。在 Step 2（詳細評估）中，應如何彌補「內部知識不足」的缺口？

  • 外部知識補充：搜尋同類 IgG1 mAb 的文獻（PubMed、PDA Journal），找相似 HCP 超標案例的處理方式
  • 客戶知識轉移：要求 Sponsor 提供其自身的 CMC 研究數據、分子穩定性檔案、之前 FDA 審查意見
  • 知識應用：委託外部專家（蛋白質生物物理學家）進行結構-活性分析，確認 OOS 對免疫原性的潛在影響
  • 結論文件化：所有知識蒐集過程與結論，納入 change control 作為返工協議草案的科學依據

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. ICH Q9(R1) 定義「以風險為基礎的決策」時，為什麼強調「知識」而不只是「數據」？兩者有何區別？
  2. 若一個返工事件是 CDMO 首次經歷，在 RKI Cycle 中處於什麼節點？應如何啟動循環？
  3. FMEA（失效模式與影響分析）在返工 Step 2 評估中，應針對哪些製程節點進行 RPN（風險優先數）排序？

本節重點回顧 Section Summary (5.0–5.5)

  • 5.0 定義基礎：Reworking（返工）= 將不符規格物料送入「製程外新步驟」。MAH 主責，監管機關最終核准。細胞與基因治療排除在外。(TR74 §5.0)
  • 5.1 優先工具：MoSCoW（M/S/C/W）以病患為核心評估返工優先順序，但必須使用組織 QMS 已核准的工具。(TR74 §5.1)
  • 5.2 核心區別：Reprocessing = 重複既有步驟（可預先授權）；Reworking = 新步驟（必須事先法規申報核准）。藥品製劑（DP）基本上只能再加工，不能返工。(TR74 §5.2)
  • 5.3 法規框架：返工必須提交 FDA PAS 或 EMA Type II Variation，在核准前不得出貨；Table 5.3-1 列出下游製程及 DP 製造中可能觸發返工的重大變更清單。(TR74 §5.3)
  • 5.4 PRA 九步驟：從 OOS 發現 → 複驗確認 → 根因調查 → PACMP 協議起草 → 送審核准 → 執行 → 評估 → 最終送審，每個閘口均需 QU 把關。(TR74 §5.4)
  • 5.5 知識與風險：RKI Cycle 建立知識↑→ 風險↓的正向循環。三種知識形式（內部、外部、應用）是 Step 2 評估的科學基礎；ICH Q9(R1) 兩大 QRM 原則要求科學依據與比例原則。(TR74 §5.5; ICH Q9(R1) §3.1–3.2)
  • CDMO 核心原則：在 CDMO 模型下，MAH（Sponsor）提交法規申報；CDMO 提供技術數據、執行製程。「先問後做」是 PRA 的核心精神，商業壓力不得凌駕無菌保證與 CQA 保護。
Part B: 5.6-5.13 | PDA Technical Report No. 74 (Revised 2026) | p45-p54

本章 Part B 學習目標

  • 理解 Post-Approval Change (PAC) 的六大決策工具，並能應用 Table 5.6-1 框架評估返工文件完整性。
  • 說明 ICH Q12 引入的 Established Conditions (EC) 概念如何改變返工事件的監管申報邏輯。
  • 掌握 Post-Approval Change Management Protocol (PACMP) 與 Comparability Protocol 的關係，以及 CDMO 如何為 Sponsor 準備此類文件。
  • 辨別返工過程中蛋白質不穩定的化學性與物理性根因，並了解 CQA 偏差 vs 分析方法干擾的鑑別原則。
  • 說明跨部門溝通計畫的關鍵要素（5.10.1 角色、5.10.2 溝通），以及台灣 CDMO 在 TFDA + US FDA + 歐盟三轄區同步申報的現實挑戰。
  • 列出典型返工時程的六個階段（共 6–12 個月），並能識別 CBE-30 vs PAS vs EU Type II Variation 的差異。
  • 說明品質部門在返工「事前把關」與「執行期間監督」的雙重角色，以及需要預先準備的文件清單。
5.6 Post-Approval Change Tools 上市後變更決策工具

原文內容 Original Text

When deciding to implement a post-approval change (PAC), thereby aiming for a new desired state, the tools suggested in Table 5.6-1 can be beneficial while drafting the documentation and scientific justifications. The use of tools and points for consideration noted in Table 5.6-1 can aid in identifying and presenting, at the outset, the most convincing and thorough documentation required for the approval process of Reworking. (See PDA Technical Report No. 91: Post-Approval Change Management and Implementation for Biologics and Pharmaceutical Drug Products–A User's Guide.)

A regulatory toolbox was jointly agreed upon by the EMA and the FDA on 26 November 2018. The agencies sought to identify scientific and regulatory solutions to challenges commonly experienced by applicants of early-access applications in completing Module 3 data requirements in time for the marketing authorization applications (MAA).

"The use of tools and points for consideration noted in Table 5.6-1 can aid in identifying and presenting, at the outset, the most convincing and thorough documentation required for the approval process of Reworking." — PDA TR74 §5.6

See Table 5.6-1 (Tools and Considerations for Decision-Making for Post-Approval Change) below — placed full-width for readability.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

Post-Approval Change (PAC，上市後變更): 任何在上市核准後對已核准製程、規格、設施或其他 CMC 要素的更動，均屬 PAC。返工本質上就是一種非預期的 PAC——它並非計畫性變更，而是因 OOS 觸發的緊急製程調整。

Table 5.6-1 六大決策維度:

  • Defining the Scope：明確變更背景與範圍
  • Understanding Risk Assessment：CQA/CPP/EC 是否受影響
  • Regulatory Assessment：風險高低決定申報類別
  • Definition / Approval Strategy：Design space 與 PACMP
  • Implementation Process：驗證、送件、報告
  • Tools：商業案例、QRM、核准策略

比喻說明 Analogy

Table 5.6-1 就像一份「建築工程變更申請書」的標準格式——建築師不能只說「我想改樓梯位置」，必須說明為什麼改、結構強度評估、主管機關許可條件、施工計畫、竣工驗收。少任何一欄，申請就退件。PAC 也是相同邏輯。

重點提示 Key Notes

FDA + EMA 聯合工具箱 (2018): EMA 與 FDA 在 2018 年 11 月正式認可共同監管工具框架，代表跨轄區申報策略可以趨同——對台灣 CDMO 而言，此框架提供了可依循的雙邊對齊基礎。然而 TFDA 尚未正式採納 ICH Q12，需確認本地規範的對應要求。

TR91 交叉參考: PDA TR74 §5.6 明確指向 PDA TR91 (Post-Approval Change Management and Implementation for Biologics)——完整 PAC 實務請參照 TR91。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. Table 5.6-1 的「Risk Assessment」欄位中，什麼情況下風險被評為「high」、須走 Prior Approval Submission？
  2. 若一間台灣 CDMO 尚未在 BLA 中建立 Established Conditions，它能否直接使用 PACMP 流程？請說明原因。

實務應用 Practical Application — CDMO 角度

你的美國 Sponsor 要求 CDMO 提交完整的 Table 5.6-1 六欄自評表作為 Tech Transfer Package 的一部分。身為 OE Manager，你需協調 MS&T（製程理解）、RA（申報策略）、QA（EC 認定）三個部門各自填具後彙整。建立一份以 Table 5.6-1 欄位為骨幹的跨部門 SOP 是最有效的準備方式。
