Table 5.6-1 解讀要點

  • 左至右 = 從問題到行動的決策流：先定義範圍 → 評估風險 → 確認監管類別 → 設計核准策略 → 執行實施。每一欄的輸出是下一欄的輸入。
  • 「EC 是否已建立」是關鍵分水嶺：若已建立 EC 且變更不影響任何 EC，可能僅需 PQS 內部管理；若 EC 受影響，則必須走正式申報。這是 ICH Q12 帶來的最大紅利——降低低風險變更的監管負擔。
  • CDMO 現實檢核：若你的 BLA（生物製品許可申請）尚未建立 EC 清單，則 Table 5.6-1 第三欄的「Q12 PAC procedure」路徑實際上無法使用。此時所有重大變更都預設走 PAS（Prior Approval Supplement）。
  • 決策層級提醒：無菌保證 > CQA 保護 > 商業彈性。當申報策略影響患者安全時，絕不以時程壓力妥協。
5.7 Established Conditions 既定條件

原文內容 Original Text

The implementation of ICH Quality Guideline Q12: Technical and Regulatory Considerations for Pharmaceutical Product Lifecycle Management by different regulatory agencies will also enable the recognition of Established Conditions (ECs) that require regulatory notification as well as those non-ECs that have been recognized as not necessary to ensure product quality and, therefore, can be managed prior to implementation notification. The amount of flexibility in a control strategy is based on the totality of product and process understanding (e.g., prior knowledge, development studies) in the context of QRM principles described in ICH Q9(R1).

A control strategy is designed to ensure that a product of required quality will be produced consistently. This planned set of controls, derived from current product and process understanding, assures process performance and product quality. The controls can include parameters and attributes related to drug substance and drug product materials and components, capability of the verified mathematical models, facility and equipment operating conditions, in-process controls, finished product specifications, and the associated methods and frequency of monitoring and control. The control strategy is based on the development of the CQAs which, in turn, have been based on thorough scientific work.

Pharmaceutical development activities result in an appropriate control strategy of the ECs, which are critical elements identified and proposed by the MAH to assure product quality and, therefore, would require a regulatory submission if changes impacted any EC. ECs can include CPPs, critical material attributes (CMAs), and CQAs as defined in ICH Q8(R2).

In the event of reworking of a drug substance or drug product, CMC changes can occur. Thus, the ECs for the manufacturing process should be defined based on enhanced product and process understanding, considering all the relevant elements of the control strategy. To identify the ECs, an enhanced approach is recommended with an increased understanding of interaction between the changed key and critical input parameters along with the outputs, and the impact on quality attributes together with a corresponding control strategy. Once ECs are identified for the material to be reworked, a detailed initial risk assessment must be developed from the prior knowledge gathered to identify the potential risk to product quality associated with changing the ECs and considering the overall control strategy.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

Established Conditions (EC，既定條件): ICH Q12 定義的 EC 是「MAH 向主管機關申報、且被核准後必須維持不變的 CMC 要素清單」。只有寫進 EC 清單的參數或屬性，才需在變更時走正式監管申報。

Non-EC vs EC:

  • EC（需申報）：例如最終滅菌過濾器孔徑、某關鍵色譜管柱品牌/型號
  • Non-EC（可 PQS 內管理）：例如非關鍵緩衝液配製順序、輔助性清洗步驟

EC 的三大組成： CPP（關鍵製程參數）、CMA（關鍵物料屬性）、CQA（關鍵品質屬性）——均源自 ICH Q8(R2) 的 QbD 架構。

比喻說明 Analogy

EC 就像一棟建築的「結構圖說」——已向政府主管機關申報備案的樑柱位置、承重牆位置都是 EC。想要移動這些元素，必須重新申請建照（監管申報）。但室內裝潢、油漆顏色就是 Non-EC，屋主自行決定即可，只需留存紀錄。

返工就像發現建築有結構偏差——要確認修繕方案是否動到備案的結構圖（EC），動到就必須向主管機關報告。

重點提示 Key Notes

ICH Q12 的革命性意義： 在 Q12 之前，幾乎所有重大製程變更都需要 PAS（Prior Approval Supplement），等待時間 6–12 個月。Q12 的 EC 框架讓「不影響 EC 的變更」可以走 CBE-30 甚至 PQS 內管理，大幅縮短時程。

台灣 CDMO 的現實挑戰： TFDA 在 2024 年以前尚未正式採納 ICH Q12。若 BLA 是美國 FDA 核准的，美國 Sponsor 期待 PACMP/EC 框架；但若同時在台灣生產供台灣市場，TFDA 可能仍要求走傳統 Type II variation 等效流程。建議與 Sponsor 的 RA 部門建立雙軌申報策略，而非單純複製美國申請。

EC 識別決策樹 EC Identification Logic

製程參數 / 物料屬性 / 品質屬性
          ↓
是否直接影響患者安全 / 產品 CQA？
    是 → 候選 EC（需申報）
    否 → 候選 Non-EC（PQS 內管理）
          ↓（對候選 EC）
是否已有足夠科學數據支持「變更不影響 CQA」？
    有 → 可能降為 Non-EC + 申報豁免
    無 → 維持 EC 狀態，變更需先驗證後申報

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 一間 CDMO 的批次製造紀錄中有 500 個製程參數。請問哪些原則決定其中哪些需要列為 EC？
  2. 返工過程中若必須變更某個「已申報的 EC」（例如超濾截留分子量從 30 kDa 改為 50 kDa），下一步應該如何處理？
5.8 Post-Approval Change Management Protocols (PACMP) 上市後變更管理協議

原文內容 Original Text

The PACMP tools described in ICH Q12 enable the planning and implementation of changes to ECs and/or CPPs, and thereby to regulatory filings, in an efficient structured manner. The PACMP (or comparability protocol) approved by the relevant health authority provides an agreement between the MAH and the regulatory agency and describes the changes and level of detail complying to the complexity, major variation, risk assessment, control strategy, and other pertinent elements. Once a PACMP is approved, when the proposed study design or acceptance criteria changes, an update of the protocol should be submitted for implementation as agreed upon in the original protocol. If changes are needed due to unanticipated or unforeseen changes in plans, prior approval of a new or revised PACMP by the regulatory agency may be required.

In the event of a reworking, the proposed comparability protocol (CP) for a modified manufacturing process should sufficiently cover the intended change and provide an increased control when compared to the existing process. A CP can be appropriately designed and/or drafted using a risk-based approach, with an in-depth or a high-level knowledge of process and product understanding. A risk assessment should be conducted on the potential drug substance and/or intermediate CQAs to be affected by parameter changes, including unspecified parameters.

Knowledge from previous developmental studies, small-scale studies, and/or pilot studies can be critical to identify potential risks to quality and provide support in the development of a suitable evaluation plan. The risk of adverse effects as a result of cumulative changes during a reworking should be carefully identified, justified, and included in the supporting information for the CP.

The reworked material should be assessed with suitable structural characterization, analytical and procedures. It should meet the criteria to demonstrate the lack of adverse effect, including immunogenicity on the reworked product quality considering the impact of structural changes in drug substance and/or drug product. Depending on the type and complexity of the drug substance, functional characterization and additional studies should also be included.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

PACMP (Post-Approval Change Management Protocol，上市後變更管理協議): MAH 與監管機構預先商定的「變更框架協議」——等同於一份「預先批准的變更藍圖」。一旦 PACMP 獲批，未來按此藍圖執行的變更可享受較快的審查路徑。

Comparability Protocol (CP，可比性協議): PACMP 的具體技術版本，描述變更後如何證明產品品質與原製程相當。必須涵蓋：分析測試計畫、接受標準、穩定性策略、免疫原性評估。

累積變更效應 (Cumulative Changes): 返工可能涉及多個製程步驟的同步調整。每一步驟單獨的風險可能低，但累積起來可能對蛋白質結構產生意外影響。CP 必須明確討論此風險。

比喻說明 Analogy

PACMP 就像預先向政府申請的「施工範圍許可令」——先核定哪些類型的修繕可以在一定範圍內自行決定，哪些需要每次個別申請。拿到許可令後，在許可範圍內施工只需備案；超出範圍才需重新申請。返工的 PACMP 意義相同：預先取得框架同意，加快事件發生時的回應速度。

重點提示 Key Notes

免疫原性是底線： 蛋白質返工最嚴格的要求之一是免疫原性評估。任何可能導致蛋白質結構改變的步驟（pH 改變、額外過濾、熱應力）都可能影響患者抗體反應，屬於患者安全考量，優先於一切商業考量。

CDMO 無 PACMP 時的實務對策：

  1. 與 Sponsor 確認現有 BLA 中是否已有核准的 PACMP 或 CP——如有，CDMO 僅需在框架內執行。
  2. 如無，CDMO 需協助 Sponsor 起草新的 CP，並預期 4–8 週的機構審查時間（CBE-30 路徑），或更長的 PAS 路徑。
  3. 此準備工作應納入 Technology Transfer 計畫的 RA 里程碑。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. PACMP 與逐案申報 (case-by-case PAS) 的主要優勢差異為何？在哪種情況下 PACMP 不適用？
  2. 返工過程中必須更換一個超濾膜（UF membrane），且此膜材未列於現有 PACMP 範圍內。請問應如何處理？

實務應用 Practical Application

Amaran 作為台灣 CDMO，若承接一個 US FDA 核准的單株抗體 DS 製造，且 Sponsor 在 BLA 中已建立 PACMP，你的工廠執行返工時應優先確認：①返工步驟是否在 PACMP 涵蓋的 EC 範圍內；②若不在範圍內，誰負責向 FDA 提交修訂版 PACMP（通常是 MAH/Sponsor，CDMO 提供技術數據支持）；③台灣本地批次若供應台灣市場，需同步向 TFDA 評估是否需要額外申報。

5.9 Instabilities and Quality Concerns 不穩定性與品質疑慮

原文內容 Original Text

Protein degradation, aggregation, poses significant challenges in the manufacturing and quality control of biologicals, particularly during reworking processes. Given that, generally, these proteins are only marginally stable in solution, they are susceptible to various forms of instability. Chemical instabilities like deamidation, oxidation, and hydrolysis, alongside such physical instabilities as denaturation and noncovalent aggregation, can compromise the quality and efficacy of the drug substances.

During an event of reworking, proteins will be exposed to stress conditions, such as elevated temperatures, low pH, or hydrophobic surfaces, which might trigger conformational instabilities. Formulation of drug substances at high concentrations can further encourage protein aggregation, impacting long-term stability.

To mitigate these risks, purification steps are essential for removing impurities and aggregates. It is crucial to implement appropriate process controls that manage pH, buffer components, and denaturants to prevent protein unfolding, which can lead to aggregation. These controls are vital to ensuring the drug substance meet specifications, maintains good appearance without visible particulates, retains stability during holding and storage, preserves efficacy, and minimizes immunogenicity concerns.

Protein manufacturing and formulation are complex processes with several factors that can impact the quality and stability of therapeutic proteins, such as:

  • Protein Concentration and Viscosity: During reworking, increased protein concentration can lead to higher viscosity, which is problematic for formulations intended for subcutaneous injections. Techniques such as rheology and dynamic light-scattering can be employed to evaluate viscosity impacts.
  • Thermal Stress: Elevated temperatures, particularly during viral inactivation steps, can lead to protein denaturation and aggregation.
  • High Ionic Strength: The use of high-ionic-strength eluents in ion-exchange and hydrophobic interaction chromatography may promote aggregation.
  • pH Considerations: Eluents with pH values near the protein's isoelectric point, or far from it, can lead to aggregation.
  • Filtration Processes: Membrane contact, presence of air bubbles, and shear stress during filtration can induce aggregation. Ultrafiltration at high protein concentrations requires careful management.
  • Formulation Challenges: Bulk storage, freeze-thaw cycles, and agitation during formulation processes can stress proteins and cause aggregation.
  • Air-Water Interfaces: Exposure to air-water interfaces during formulation can promote aggregate formation by lowering the energy barrier for protein unfolding.
  • Excipients in Formulation: Certain excipients can stress proteins and accelerate aggregation. For instance, magnesium ions (Mg²⁺) have been noted for their potential to increase aggregation rates in some formulations.
  • Visible Particulates: It is critical to effectively monitor visible particulates after any reworking.
  • Leachables and Extractables: Detected in various sterilizing-grade filters (PVDF, PES, mixed cellulose ester). These demonstrate complex patterns of destabilizing and stabilizing effects on the physical and chemical stability of mAbs, including formation of visible and subvisible particles.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

蛋白質不穩定性的兩大類型：

化學性不穩定 (Chemical Instability):

  • 去醯胺化 (Deamidation)：Asn/Gln 側鏈水解，影響電荷分佈
  • 氧化 (Oxidation)：Met/Trp/Cys 被氧化，影響結合活性
  • 水解 (Hydrolysis)：肽鍵斷裂，產生碎片

物理性不穩定 (Physical Instability):

  • 變性 (Denaturation)：三維結構展開，喪失活性
  • 非共價聚集 (Noncovalent Aggregation)：可逆或不可逆聚集體，觸發免疫反應風險
  • 纖維化 (Fibrillation)：有序聚集結構，高免疫原性

比喻說明 Analogy

蛋白質分子就像精密折紙藝術品——正確折疊的三維結構才有功能。返工中的額外製程步驟像是把折紙重新處理：pH 偏移是用水泡折紙（紙張膨脹變形）、高溫是烘乾（結構收縮），震盪是反覆折疊（疲勞斷裂）。每一步都有可能讓折紙永久變形而無法還原。

重點提示 Key Notes

區分真正的不穩定 vs 分析方法干擾： 返工後若 SEC-HPLC 顯示聚集體增加，應先確認：①樣品前處理是否引入了人工聚集？②分析方法是否已驗證在此返工樣品基質中的適用性？③是否同步做了強制降解（forced degradation）對照？排除分析干擾後，才能將結果解讀為真實品質偏差。

Leachables & Extractables 的新興警示： PVDF 和 PES 等滅菌級過濾膜的可溶出物可能對 mAb 產生「界面活性劑效應」，加速蛋白質聚集。返工中若引入新的過濾器接觸材料，必須進行 L&E 評估——這是 §5.11 時程中「Analytical Testing (4–8 週)」的重要項目。

決策層級警示： 免疫原性風險 = 患者安全直接威脅 → 永遠優先於生產時程或成本考量（決策層級第一位）。

返工後不穩定性風險矩陣

應力因子         主要風險          關鍵監控指標
──────────────────────────────────────────────
高溫（病毒滅活） 聚集、脫醯胺      SEC-HPLC、DLS
低 pH（病毒滅活） 聚集、沉澱        外觀、濁度
高離子強度（層析）聚集、蛋白質沉澱  SEC、icIEF
超濾（高濃度）    黏度、聚集         黏度計、粒徑
凍融循環          聚集、可見微粒    粒子計數、外觀
震盪              表面吸附聚集       外觀、SEC

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 返工過程中蛋白質聚集體突然增加，第一步應如何判斷是「製程導致的真實聚集」還是「分析方法偽陽性」？
  2. 若在返工後的超濾步驟引入了一個新的 PVDF 膜，需要做哪些額外測試才能確認批次可接受？
5.10 Roles and Communication 角色分工與溝通

原文內容 Original Text

People drive reworking projects and ensure timely delivery of the biological drug product to the patient. Top management plays a critical role by setting the strategic direction and ensuring that all processes adhere to regulatory standards. Meanwhile, other team members can focus on operational aspects, ensuring each function, whether it is research, development, manufacturing, quality, logistics, or support, is executed efficiently.

5.10.1 Roles

Roles can be defined individually or integrated into teams, which allows for flexibility in management and execution, ultimately contributing to successful outcomes for the project and timely delivery to the patient.

Their responsibilities include:

  • Providing Strategic Direction and Oversight: Approving the rework plan, scope, and objectives; ensuring alignment with organizational goals, regulatory requirements, and quality standards.
  • Ensuring Regulatory Compliance and Risk Management: Supporting adherence to GMP, regulatory guidelines, and internal SOPs; overseeing risk assessments and mitigation strategies.
  • Allocating Resources and Budget: Approving necessary budgets, personnel, facilities, and equipment; ensuring sufficient resources for effective execution.
  • Facilitating Cross-Functional Collaboration: Promoting communication among manufacturing, QA, regulatory, and other departments. Departments should explicitly include contract manufacturers responsible for intermediates and supply chain/demand planning teams, and manufacturing resilience given their impact on production scheduling, inventory, and communication with commercial functions.
  • Monitoring Progress and Performance: Receiving regular updates on status, challenges, and outcomes; making high-level decisions to address issues or deviations promptly.
  • Ensuring Regulatory Submissions and Documentation: Approving documentation for regulatory filings, deviations, or change controls associated with reworking; ensuring thorough documentation for compliance and traceability.
  • Managing Ethical and Safety Considerations: Prioritizing patient safety and product quality; supporting a culture of transparency and accountability.
  • Post-Rework Evaluation and Continuous Improvement: Reviewing rework outcomes including quality, stability, and regulatory feedback; implementing lessons learned to improve future processes.

5.10.2 Communication

Effective communication is essential to ensure that all stakeholders are informed, coordinated, and aligned throughout the reworking process. The best approach involves a structured, transparent, and timely communication strategy. Key principles and steps:

  • Develop a Communication Plan: Define objectives, identify stakeholders (internal: Quality, Manufacturing, R&D, RA, Management; external: regulators, partners, suppliers), establish channels, set frequency.
  • Ensure Transparency and Clarity: Articulate reasons for rework, potential impacts, and actions being taken. Communicate known risks and mitigation strategies upfront.
  • Maintain Documentation and Traceability: Record all communications, decisions, and approvals. Use controlled documents and logs.
  • Facilitate Cross-Functional Collaboration: Hold regular cross-disciplinary meetings. Encourage open dialogue to surface concerns early.
  • Implement Regulatory Communication Protocols: If rework impacts product quality or regulatory filings, prepare necessary documentation for regulators.
  • Designate Clear Roles and Responsibilities: Assign communication responsibilities to specific personnel (e.g., project manager, Quality head, process science/MSAT head).
  • Use Clear, Concise, and Consistent Messaging: Avoid technical jargon when communicating with nonexperts. Ensure messages are consistent across all channels.
  • Prepare for Crisis or Unexpected Events: Develop contingency communication plans for contamination, delays, or regulatory findings.

The best approach to communication management during reworking is a proactive, transparent, and well-structured strategy that involves developing a detailed communication plan, ensuring cross-functional collaboration, maintaining thorough documentation, and engaging regulatory authorities when needed.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts — 5.10.1 角色

返工事件的典型跨功能團隊 (Cross-Functional Team, CFT)：

  • QA（品質保證）：最終決策者、變更控制負責人、偏差調查主導
  • QC（品質控制）：額外分析測試執行、結果解讀
  • MS&T / Process Science（製程科學）：返工步驟設計、小規模研究、技術評估
  • RA（法規事務）：申報策略、與主管機關溝通、文件準備
  • MFG（製造）：執行返工操作、記錄偏差
  • Supply Chain：原料可用性、排程影響、商業團隊溝通
  • Sponsor（委託方）：最終策略決定、資源核准

特別注意：TR74 明確點名合約製造商 (CMO) 與供應鏈/需求規劃團隊應納入跨部門協作——此條文直接指向 CDMO 應主動融入 Sponsor 的決策循環，而非被動等待指令。

核心概念解析 Key Concepts — 5.10.2 溝通

返工溝通計畫的七要素：

  1. 溝通目標（What）
  2. 利害關係人清單（Who）
  3. 溝通頻率（When）
  4. 溝通管道（How）——正式 vs 非正式
  5. 文件追溯性（Traceability）
  6. 監管溝通協議（Regulatory Communication Protocol）
  7. 危機溝通預案（Contingency Plan）

比喻說明 Analogy

返工的跨部門溝通就像急救手術的「手術室簡報 (surgical huddle)」——開始前 5 分鐘，主刀、麻醉師、護理師、器械師各自確認分工與風險。沒有清晰的角色分工，手術就容易出錯。CDMO 的返工決策會議應比照此標準——不能只有 QA 一人講、其他人沉默。

重點提示 Key Notes — CDMO 跨組織溝通挑戰

台灣 CDMO 執行返工時，溝通的複雜度高於自有產品廠：

  • 語言差異：美國 Sponsor 的技術溝通以英文為主，內部溝通以中文進行，翻譯準確性影響決策品質。
  • 時差：台北與美東時差 12–13 小時，緊急返工決策需建立非工作時間溝通協議（oncall protocol）。
  • 授權層級：某些變更決策需 Sponsor 的 QA 或 RA VP 批准，CDMO 不能單獨決定。提前明確授權矩陣 (RACI) 可防止返工執行延誤。
  • 保密協議：返工涉及 Sponsor 的 IP（製程機密），所有溝通紀錄需符合 CDA/MSA 規定。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 返工事件發生時，誰應該被列為「必須在 24 小時內通知」的關鍵利害關係人？請從 CDMO 角度建立優先清單。
  2. 若 Sponsor 的 RA 部門與 CDMO 的 QA 部門對返工風險評估有不同意見，決策權在誰？如何解決分歧？

實務應用 Practical Application

建議在 Tech Transfer 階段即建立「返工溝通矩陣 (Rework Communication Matrix)」，明定：①事件分類標準（輕微 / 嚴重）；②各類事件的通知時限（例：嚴重 OOS 4 小時內通知 Sponsor QA Director）；③正式溝通管道（email cc 清單 + 電話備援）；④決策授權層級（哪些決策 CDMO 可自行決定，哪些需 Sponsor 批准）。此矩陣應納入 Quality Agreement (QAA) 附件。

5.11 Submission & Approval Timelines 送件與核准時程

原文內容 Original Text

Reworking a biological drug substance involves carefully revisiting and potentially modifying production processes to ensure product quality, safety, and efficacy. The timeline for reworking such a drug substance and/or drug product can vary significantly depending on several factors, including the complexity of the product, extent of modifications needed, regulatory requirements, and manufacturing facility's capabilities.

Typical phases and approximate timelines:

  1. Assessment and Planning (2–4 weeks): Evaluation of the current process and product; identifying reasons for rework; developing a detailed rework plan and risk assessment.
  2. Process Development and Optimization (4–12 weeks): Adjusting upstream or downstream processes; small-scale laboratory or pilot studies; analytical method development or validation if needed.
  3. Analytical and Stability Testing (4–8 weeks): Confirming product integrity, potency, and purity post-rework; stability testing to ensure product remains within specifications.
  4. Scale-up and Validation (8–16 weeks): Manufacturing at larger scale; process validation batches to confirm reproducibility.
  5. Regulatory Documentation and Submission (4–12 weeks): Preparing amendments or supplemental dossiers; addressing agency queries and obtaining prior approval.
  6. Manufacturing and Release (2–6 weeks, variable): Final production run; quality release-testing and documentation.
"Total Estimated Timeline: Typically, reworking a drug substance can take approximately 6 to 12 months, but in some cases, especially with complex modifications or regulatory hurdles, it may extend longer." — PDA TR74 §5.11

Factors Influencing Reworking Timeline:

  • Regulatory Pathways: The need for prior approval or additional filings can significantly affect timelines. Approval processes differ by region.
  • Extent of Process Changes: More extensive changes require deeper assessments and validation efforts.
  • Availability of Raw Materials and Manufacturing Capacity: Supply chain considerations and manufacturing capacity can cause delays.
  • Quality and Analytical Testing Turnaround Times: Time for quality and analytical testing can impact timelines, especially if retesting is required.
  • Single-use Systems: If new single-use systems with greater process contact-surface area or new polymers are introduced, a detailed leachable and extractable impact assessment will need to be performed before execution.
  • Regulatory Agency Review Times: Variability in how long agencies take to review submissions and respond can introduce uncertainties.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts — 申報路徑對照

美國 FDA 三種申報路徑（生物製品 BLA）：

  • Prior Approval Supplement (PAS)：上市前需獲核准，FDA 目標審查時限 6 個月（一般）或 2 個月（急件）。適用：高風險製程變更、CQA 可能受影響。
  • Changes Being Effected in 30 Days (CBE-30)：提交後 30 天可實施（FDA 如無反對）。適用：中度風險變更。
  • Annual Report (AR)：年度彙整申報，實施前不需等待。適用：低風險、輕微變更。

歐盟 EMA 主要路徑：

  • Type II Variation（主要變更）：審查時限 60 天（有效時限），對應 FDA PAS，高風險製程變更。
  • Type IB Variation（中度變更）：30 天通知後可實施，對應 FDA CBE-30。
  • Type IA (IAIN, 立即通知) / 年度評估：對應 FDA Annual Report。

返工時程估算框架

階段                          時間範圍
─────────────────────────────────────
1. 評估與規劃                  2–4 週
2. 製程開發與優化              4–12 週
3. 分析與穩定性測試            4–8 週
4. 放大與驗證                  8–16 週
5. 監管文件準備與送件          4–12 週
   ├─ CBE-30：送出後 30 天
   ├─ PAS：等待 6–12 個月*
   └─ EU Type II：等待 2–6 個月
6. 製造與放行                  2–6 週
─────────────────────────────────────
總計（不含監管等待）：        24–58 週
最終總時程（含 PAS 等待）：   6–18 個月
*急件 PAS 可申請加速審查 (2 個月目標)

比喻說明 Analogy

返工時程就像飛機緊急迫降後的「適航性恢復計畫」——工程師評估損傷（第 1 階段）→ 設計修復方案並小規模測試（第 2 階段）→ 完整結構測試（第 3 階段）→ 試飛驗證（第 4 階段）→ 向民航局申請恢復飛行許可（第 5 階段）→ 正式投入服務（第 6 階段）。跳過任何一步，民航局就不會發許可。製藥返工的監管邏輯完全相同。

重點提示 Key Notes

CDMO 時程規劃的三大陷阱：

  1. 低估監管等待時間：若返工需 PAS（FDA）+ Type II Variation（EMA），兩個機構同時送件，平行審查仍可能需要 6–12 個月。不能假設所有市場可同步獲批。
  2. Leachables & Extractables 測試時間：若引入新的一次性系統（Single-Use）接觸材料，L&E 研究本身可能需要 8–16 週，必須提前納入計畫。
  3. 穩定性數據缺口：返工批次需要至少初期穩定性數據（通常 3 個月）才能支持申報文件。穩定性研究必須在最終放大驗證批完成後立即啟動。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 一個返工案例涉及將色譜管柱樹脂從 A 品牌換成 B 品牌（相同樹脂類型，不同廠商）。在美國 FDA BLA 框架下，此變更最可能走哪一種申報路徑？理由為何？
  2. 若返工完成後，Sponsor 希望在 4 個月內恢復供應，你的 Project Manager 詢問「能否在監管核准前先製造批次等待放行？」請從 GMP 和監管合規角度回答此問題。
5.12 Quality Unit Preparedness 品質部門的預備狀態

原文內容 Original Text

The Quality Unit requires comprehensive training documents to ensure compliance and efficiency during unexpected events of reworking. Typical documents that might be needed:

  • Standard Operating Procedures (SOPs): SOPs for rework processes with step-by-step instructions; SOPs for identifying and segregating nonconforming materials.
  • Regulatory Guidelines: Relevant regulatory guidelines from FDA, EMA, or other local/national standards related to rework.
  • Quality Control Procedures: Documents detailing quality control checks required before, during, and after rework.
  • Safety Training Documents: Training materials on safety procedures specific to rework operations.
  • Documentation and Recordkeeping Training: Instructions for accurate documentation and recordkeeping to ensure traceability and compliance.
  • Risk Assessment and Management: Guidelines for conducting risk assessments related to reworking processes.
  • Material Handling Procedures: Proper procedures for handling materials safely during the rework process.
  • Equipment Handling and Maintenance: Training on specific equipment used for reworking, including maintenance and calibration.
  • Continuous Improvement Practices: Documents that facilitate identifying areas for improvement in rework processes.

Steps to effectively prepare for a reworking event:

  1. Risk Assessment and Planning: Conduct thorough risk assessment; prepare detailed rework plan with objectives, resources, timelines, and personnel responsibilities.
  2. Documentation and SOPs: Ensure all SOPs related to rework are up to date; document every step clearly and maintain traceability.
  3. Training: Provide training for personnel involved in reworking activities on new procedures, equipment use, and quality requirements.
  4. Material Management: Review and inspect raw materials, components, and consumables; establish segregation system for nonconforming materials.
  5. Monitoring, Review, and Control: Set up monitoring and control mechanisms; implement checks and balances to detect deviations promptly.
  6. Communication: Maintain clear communication channels within the team and with other departments.
  7. Quality Assurance: Conduct QA checks before, during, and after the rework. The quality unit is ultimately responsible for ensuring product quality and providing quality oversight throughout any reworking activity.
  8. Feedback and Improvement: After completing the rework, gather feedback and conduct thorough process review to identify improvement areas; update policies and procedures to reflect lessons learned.

It is crucial for the quality unit, comprising both quality assurance and quality control, to be well-prepared to manage the situations effectively and ensure that product quality and compliance are maintained. Ultimately, preparedness involves a combination of detailed planning, ongoing training, and resource management and ensuring that the team is proactive in adapting to any new challenges that arise during the reworking process.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

品質部門的雙重角色：

① 事前把關 (Pre-Approval Gating)： 在返工方案提交監管機構前，QU 是最終技術與法規審核的把關者——未獲 QU 批准的返工協議不得送件，更不得執行。

② 執行期間監督 (During-Execution Oversight)： 返工批次的每一個關鍵步驟（pH 調整、溫度控制、過濾操作）都需 QA 現場或遠端即時監督，QC 須執行即時分析以提供決策數據。

QA vs QC 分工：

  • QA：系統合規性、偏差管理、批次放行決策
  • QC：分析測試執行、OOS 調查、方法適用性確認

比喻說明 Analogy

品質部門的返工預備工作就像消防站的「災害應變演練」——消防員不能等到火災發生才開始學習操作消防車。返工 SOP、不符合物料隔離程序、緊急分析方法——都必須在平時演練好、文件備妥。當返工事件真正發生時，QU 的工作是「執行已訓練的程序」而非「臨時學習新技能」。

重點提示 Key Notes

「事前準備」的五個關鍵文件清單（CDMO 具體版）：

  1. 返工決策矩陣 SOP：定義哪些偏差可考慮返工、哪些應直接拒絕——防止返工成為「逃避拒批的捷徑」。
  2. 不符合物料隔離程序：返工中間物必須與正常批次完全實體隔離，並有明確標識。
  3. 額外分析方法清單：預先識別哪些 ECLs（延伸特性測試）可能需要用到——例如 SEC-HPLC 聚集體分析、icIEF 電荷異質性。
  4. 穩定性研究啟動標準作業：返工批次完成後，穩定性研究必須即時啟動，不得延遲。
  5. Sponsor 通知程序：符合 QAA 要求的通知時限與格式，需預先建立模板。

返工 QU 監督檢查點

返工階段           QA 責任                QC 責任
──────────────────────────────────────────────────
事前（批准前）    審核返工協議           確認方法適用性
                  批准 PACMP 送件        準備額外測試方法

執行中            現場 / 遠端監督        即時分析（IPC）
                  偏差即時記錄           OOS 快速評估
                  關鍵步驟簽批           特性分析測試

執行後            批次記錄審核           穩定性樣品取樣
                  與 RA 協調送件         ECL 測試執行
                  批次放行決策           分析數據審核

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 如果你今天被要求評估貴廠對於一個「mAb DS 色譜步驟 OOS → 考慮返工」事件的 QU 準備度，你會優先查看哪三份文件的現況？
  2. 在返工執行期間，QC 發現一個中間體測試結果超出 Action Level（但未超出規格）。QA 應如何決策？是否繼續、停止或調查後再決定？

實務應用 Practical Application

建議每年進行一次「返工桌上演練 (Rework Table-Top Exercise)」——模擬一個典型 mAb DS 批次的 OOS 場景，讓 QA、QC、MS&T、RA、MFG 各部門代表走過完整的決策流程。桌上演練的輸出是一份「準備度缺口評估報告」，用以識別文件缺失、人員能力不足、或跨部門溝通盲點，並轉化為 CAPA。這是最具成本效益的返工準備投資。

5.13 Conclusions 結論

原文內容 Original Text

In urgent situations, such as a global pandemic (e.g., COVID-19), wars, or natural disasters (e.g., Category 5 hurricanes, catastrophic earthquakes, major floods, meteor catastrophe), certain regulatory flexibilities or deviations may be considered by the MAH to address critical supply issues, like immediate drug shortages. However, reworking an OOS drug substance generally involves significant quality and regulatory considerations, such as:

  • Regulatory Frameworks and Guidance: Regulatory agencies such as the U.S. FDA, EMA, and other agencies offer guidance on managing deviations, OOS results, and manufacturing challenges. In urgent situations, these agencies may provide tailored guidance or emergency procedures. However, deviations from approved specifications generally require proper justification and thorough documentation.
  • Reworking of OOS Drug Substance: Reworking involves processing material that initially failed to meet specifications to bring it into compliance. This process must be validated and scientifically justified, demonstrating that reworking does not compromise product quality, safety, stability and efficacy.
  • Regulatory Approval and Documentation: Any decision to rework should be thoroughly documented, including risk assessments and validation data. For licensed products, regulatory authorities often require that deviations or exceptions from established processes be reported. Depending on the jurisdiction and the specific nature and impact of the change, prior approval may be necessary.
  • Risk Management and Justification: In emergencies or shortages, regulators may offer some flexibility, but the company must ensure reworking does not compromise drug quality. A comprehensive risk assessment, incorporating knowledge management, should be conducted to evaluate its impact on safety and efficacy.
  • Good Manufacturing Practice Compliance: Reworking must adhere to GMP standards, and the process should be validated. Proper change control procedures should be followed.
"Reworking an OOS drug substance should never be treated as routine. However, in urgent situations such as a pandemic or critical shortage, biotechnology companies may consider reworking if it is properly justified, validated, and documented. They should proactively engage with regulatory authorities, possibly under emergency use or contingency provisions, to ensure compliance and maintain product integrity." — PDA TR74 §5.13

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

緊急情況下的監管彈性 (Regulatory Flexibility in Emergencies): COVID-19 期間，FDA 和 EMA 均發布了緊急指南，允許在特定條件下對製程進行例外偏差——但這並非「無需申報」的免責，而是「加速審查 + 後續補件」的程序調整。監管彈性的前提仍是患者安全不受損。

「絕不視為例行程序」的核心意涵： 返工從本質上是一個例外事件 (exception event)。若某工廠每批次都在考慮返工，這已不是返工問題，而是根本製程能力不足的系統性問題——必須走 CAPA，從根因改善，而非重複申請返工核准。

比喻說明 Analogy

返工就像外科手術中的「緊急處置方案」——有時必要，但絕不應是計劃外手術的常態。若一個醫院每週都要對同一類手術採取「緊急處置」，問題不在緊急處置程序，而在術前評估和手術規範本身。製藥返工的哲學完全相同：準備好應對，但以避免為目標。

重點提示 Key Notes — 積極主動的心態 (Proactive Mindset)

TR74 §5.13 傳遞的核心訊息——預防勝於應對：

  • 提前建立 PACMP：不要等到 OOS 發生才起草——這就像只有在火災發生時才去申請消防許可。
  • 定期 EC 審查：每年與 Sponsor 和 RA 確認現有 EC 清單是否反映當前製程實際狀況。
  • 主動接觸主管機關：TR74 明確建議「proactively engage with regulatory authorities」——在問題擴大前主動諮詢，比被動應對更有效。對台灣 CDMO 而言，這意味著與 Sponsor 共同主動尋求 FDA/EMA 的非正式溝通 (Type C meeting, 科學諮詢)。
  • CAPA 文化優先：每一次返工事件結束後，根本原因分析和 CAPA 計畫應視為強制性輸出，而非可選項。防止重複發生是最有效的長期成本控制。

Section 5 Part B 總結 — 決策層級最終確認

回顧 Section 5 (Part B) 整章，每一個主題都指向相同的核心決策框架：

無菌保證 (Sterility) > CQA 保護 (Patient Safety) > 商業彈性 (Business)

  • §5.6–5.8：即使有 PACMP 和 EC 彈性，絕不以降低 CQA 標準換取申報速度。
  • §5.9：蛋白質不穩定和免疫原性風險是患者安全的直接威脅，優先於一切。
  • §5.10：溝通透明是維護患者安全的信任基礎，不得因商業壓力壓縮。
  • §5.11–5.12：時程再緊，也不能跳過驗證和 QU 把關。
  • §5.13：緊急彈性是工具，不是漏洞——患者安全永遠不妥協。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 你的工廠在過去 12 個月內對同一個 DS 製程發生了 3 次返工。Top Management 認為這是正常的「製程調整」。你作為 QA Manager 應如何回應，並採取哪些具體行動？
  2. 台灣發生重大地震，某 mAb DS 批次因停電導致冷鏈中斷，品質狀況不確定。Sponsor 要求 CDMO 立即評估是否可以「緊急返工」以避免藥品短缺。第一步應如何處理，而不是直接開始返工？

Section 5 Part B 重點回顧

  • PAC 六大決策維度（§5.6）：Table 5.6-1 提供了從定義範圍到執行實施的完整框架——每一個返工案例都應能在此框架中找到對應位置。
  • ICH Q12 的 EC 革命（§5.7）：Established Conditions 的建立是降低監管申報負擔的關鍵前提。若 BLA 尚未建立 EC，所有重大返工預設走 PAS 路徑。
  • PACMP = 預先取得的授權（§5.8）：一份事前獲批的 PACMP 在返工事件發生時可節省數月時間——這是最有價值的 RA 預防性投資。Comparability Protocol 必須覆蓋免疫原性評估。
  • 蛋白質不穩定十大風險因子（§5.9）：從濃度/黏度到 Leachables & Extractables，每一個返工新步驟都可能引入新的應力——必須用適當的分析工具預先評估。
  • CDMO 的跨組織溝通挑戰（§5.10）：返工不是 CDMO 的內部事務——Sponsor、監管機構、供應鏈都是必要利害關係人。溝通矩陣和 RACI 應寫入 Quality Agreement。
  • 6–12 個月的現實時程（§5.11）：PAS 等待期可能長達 12 個月；L&E 研究可能額外增加 8–16 週。早期規劃、早期送件是縮短總時程的唯一方法。
  • 品質部門雙重角色（§5.12）：QU 既是事前把關者（不批准就不送件），也是執行期間的監督者。返工 SOP、隔離程序、額外分析方法都需在平時準備好。
  • 積極主動的心態（§5.13）：返工應對是最後一道防線；預防——通過健全的製程驗證、EC 建立和 PACMP——才是正道。每一次返工事件必須以 CAPA 收尾，防止重複發生。
6

Section 6: Appendix I: AEX Reprocessing Case Study

附錄一:陰離子交換層析再處理案例 | p55-p74

PDA Technical Report No. 74 (Revised 2026) | p55 - p67

本章學習目標

  • 理解 Anion Exchange Chromatography (AEX, 陰離子交換層析) 作為 mAb 純化平台工具的單元操作特性，以及其在 HCP、DNA 清除上的關鍵角色。
  • 掌握 6.2 Points to Consider（考量要點）：Column Packing、Cleaning/Sanitization、Performance、Regeneration/Lifecycle、Validation/Filings 五個評估維度，判斷再處理的技術可行性。
  • 運用 FMEA（Failure Mode and Effects Analysis, 失效模式與影響分析）工具，以 RPN = Severity × Occurrence × Detection 系統性評分，識別 AEX 步驟為最高風險候選再處理步驟（RPN = 125）。
  • 建立再處理的商業決策框架（Option 1 廢棄批次 vs Option 2 重新設計 vs Option 3 再處理），理解 Option 3 在品質與成本之間的平衡邏輯。
  • 熟悉 6.4 Quality Considerations 中的可比性標準（Comparability Criteria）、分析方法矩陣（Analytical Methods）及監控觸發點（Monitor Triggers），作為再處理決策的品質把關依據。
6.0 Appendix I: Hypothetical Case Study (Reprocessing Framework) — Anion Exchange Chromatography 附錄一：假設性案例研究（再處理框架）— 陰離子交換層析

原文內容 Original Text

Section 6.0 (Appendix I) focuses on the design and implementation considerations for a reprocessing step. Adapted from the published monoclonal antibody manufacturing (mAb) process, A-Mab: A Case Study in Bioprocess Development, for this case study, a reprocessing framework has been created using an anion exchange chromatography (AEX) step (19). This reprocessing framework is intentionally designed to require a more comprehensive analysis than a simpler reprocessing step, such as refiltration described in Section 7.0.

Reprocessing of a major unit operation, such as an AEX chromatography column, requires a detailed assessment, significant resources, planning, and commitment. Simpler unit operations require a subset of the planning and activities outlined here. Regardless, quality management systems, regulatory requirements, and a comprehensive process understanding should drive the overall design of the reprocessing procedure.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

Reprocessing（再處理）：將不符合中間品 (intermediate) 規格的批次，在相同製程步驟重新處理一次，以達到可接受的品質標準。與 Reworking（重新加工，改用不同方法）不同。

AEX（Anion Exchange Chromatography，陰離子交換層析）：利用蛋白質表面負電荷與陽性樹脂之間的靜電作用進行分離。mAb 在 flow-through 模式下直接通過，而 HCP（Host Cell Proteins，宿主細胞蛋白）、DNA、內毒素、病毒等帶負電雜質則吸附於樹脂上被清除。

A-Mab Case Study：業界標竿性的假設性 mAb 生產案例，由多家公司聯合撰寫，廣泛用於 CMC 開發框架示範。TR74 借用此框架設計 AEX 再處理情境。

比喻說明 Analogy

AEX 再處理就像工廠品管員在出貨前發現某批零件表面殘留油污超標（相當於 HCP 超標），不是直接廢棄這批零件，而是把整批零件再送一次清洗線重新清洗。但這麼做必須先確認：清洗設備還在規格範圍內嗎？清洗次數有沒有超過驗證上限？清洗後零件品質不會變差？——這就是 6.2 Points to Consider 要回答的問題。

重點提示 Key Notes

TR74 刻意選擇 AEX 作為示範案例，因為它比「重新過濾」（Section 7.0 refiltration）更複雜：涉及樹脂壽命、柱床完整性、病毒清除驗證等多個面向。熟悉本節後，處理較簡單的再處理步驟時只需套用其子集即可。

決策層級提醒：品質管理系統與法規要求永遠優先於商業考量。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. AEX 是 flow-through 模式還是 bind-and-elute 模式？這對再處理設計有什麼影響？
  2. 為什麼 TR74 要用「假設性」案例（hypothetical case study）而非真實批次資料？
6.1 Unit Operation Characteristics 單元操作特性

原文內容 Original Text

Chromatography is used to purify a product (e.g., mAb, target proteins, compounds) considering the properties of the target solute, feed stream, required purity level, productivity, costs, process sequence, process parameters, and implementation of the designed purification process. Biomolecules are purified using chromatography techniques that separate them according to the difference in their specific properties as summarized in Table 6.1-1. In ion exchange chromatography (IEX), biomolecules are separated according to the difference in their net surface charges.

See Table 6.1-1 (Chromatography Techniques) and Table 6.1-2 (Quality Attribute Risk Assessment Topics) below.

The overall goal of a chromatographic step is to remove impurities, such as host-cell-derived proteins (HCP), nucleic acids, carbohydrates, and other undesired compounds.

In general, a full-scale chromatography system will consist of the following components:

  • Buffer and Product Reservoirs: Containers (hard-piped or single use disposables) used to supply the buffers, product feed, and for elution collection required during the chromatography operation.
  • Pumps: Peristaltic pumps used to feed the buffers into chromatography columns. Depending on scale, other types of pumps may be utilized considering process requirements and equipment design.
  • Column: The chamber where the chromatographic media is loaded. The size (diameter and height) of the column will be defined based on the process requirements. The material of construction (e.g., glass, polycarbonate, steel) is selected based on process conditions (e.g., pressure and flow rates).
  • Resin: Chromatography media intended for the purification process. The packaging of the columns is commonly conducted by creating a slurry where the particles are suspended, that is, poured into the column.
  • Valves: Sanitary systems used to control the flow of materials during the operation of the chromatography system. These may be manual or pneumatic units.
  • Sensors: Applications intended to monitor process parameters required for the chromatography process. These may include pH, air, temperature, flow, pressure, and UV monitor.
  • Controller/Computer: Used to control and monitor the operation of the system.

The purification strategy involving a chromatography step is based on the characteristics (e.g., properties and stability) of the product under different conditions, final specifications, feed properties (e.g., concentration of product and impurities), nature of the process (e.g., continuous or discontinuous), and nature of the substances (e.g., hazardous). When designing the reprocessing step for the AEX chromatography case study, consideration was given to the quality attributes for mAbs listed in Table 6.1-2 (19).

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

四大層析原理（見 Table 6.1-1）：

  • 電荷（Charge）→ IEX：AEX（陰離子交換）、CEX（陽離子交換）
  • 大小（Size）→ SEC：Size Exclusion Chromatography，用於聚集體分析
  • 疏水性（Hydrophobicity）→ HIC / RPC：Hydrophobic Interaction / Reversed Phase Chromatography
  • 生物辨識（Biorecognition）→ Affinity：Protein A 親和層析為 mAb 第一步純化主力

Flow-Through Mode（流穿模式）：AEX 通常以 flow-through 操作。mAb 在目標 pH/conductivity 下帶正電或中性，不與陰離子樹脂結合，直接流過；而 HCP、DNA、內毒素帶負電，吸附於樹脂，藉此清除雜質。這與 Protein A（bind-and-elute 模式）截然不同。

重點提示 Key Notes

Table 6.1-2 關鍵品質屬性（CQA）標記（*）：Aggregation、Galactose content、Afucosylation、High mannose content、Nonglycosylated heavy chain、Sialic acid content、Host-cell proteins (HCP)、DNA 均被標記為 CQA。再處理設計必須證明對這些 CQA 無不良影響，這是監管機關的核心關注點。

DS（Drug Substance，原料藥）層次：本案例為 DS/上游純化流程，與 DP（Drug Product，製劑）的無菌充填不同，但相同的品質風險管理邏輯適用。CDMO 在與 Sponsor 或 DS CMO 討論時，此框架提供共同語言。

比喻說明 Analogy

把層析柱想像成濾水器的濾芯，不同濾芯設計攔截不同種類的雜質（依大小、電荷、疏水性或特異性識別）。AEX 的 flow-through 模式就像用帶負電的濾網：帶負電的雜質（HCP、DNA）會被吸住，而目標蛋白（mAb）帶正電，直接通過濾網，達到純化目的。

實務應用 Practical Application

對於 Fill-Finish CDMO 而言，雖然 AEX 屬於 DS 端製程，但在 Tech Transfer 審查 DS CMO 的 Manufacturing Process Description（Section 3.2.S.2.2）時，了解 AEX 的 flow-through 原理與 HCP 清除機制，有助於評估 Sponsor 提供的 CQA 合理性及批次放行規格的風險等級。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. AEX 在 flow-through 模式下，若進料溶液的 pH 或電導率（conductivity）超出設定範圍，HCP 清除效果會如何改變？
  2. Table 6.1-2 中，哪些 CQA 與 AEX 步驟最直接相關？為什麼 HCP 和 DNA 被列為 CQA？

Table 6.1-1: Chromatography Techniques 層析技術分類

Property 分離依據 Techniques 層析技術
Charge 電荷 Ion exchange chromatography（離子交換層析，IEX）— includes AEX & CEX
Size 大小 Size exclusion chromatography（尺寸排阻層析，SEC），also called gel filtration
Hydrophobicity 疏水性 Hydrophobic interaction chromatography（疏水性相互作用層析，HIC）; Reversed phase chromatography（逆相層析，RPC）
Biorecognition (ligand specificity) 生物辨識（配體特異性） Affinity chromatography（親和層析）— e.g., Protein A for mAb capture

Table 6.1-2: Summary of Quality Attribute Risk Assessment Topics 品質屬性風險評估主題摘要

Product Quality Attributes 產品品質屬性 （* = Considered CQA 關鍵品質屬性）
Aggregation* （聚集體） Galactose content* （半乳糖含量） Afucosylation* （去岩藻糖基化）
Oxidation （氧化） Protein A （Protein A 殘留） High mannose content* （高甘露糖含量）
Nonglycosylated heavy chain* （非醣基化重鏈） C-terminal lysine （C 端離胺酸） Deamidated isoforms （去醯胺異構體）
Host-cell proteins* (HCP, 宿主細胞蛋白) Sialic acid content* （唾液酸含量） DNA （宿主細胞 DNA）
Methotrexate （甲胺蝶呤，製程殘留） —

* Considered CQA — 標記星號者為關鍵品質屬性，再處理必須確保不對其產生不良影響。

6.2 Points to Consider 考量要點

原文內容 Original Text

The elements in Section 6.2 should be considered as part of reprocessing a chromatography column. These elements are further discussed in PDA Technical Report No. 14 (Revised 2008): Validation of Column-Based Chromatography Processes for the Purification of Proteins.

6.2.1 Column Packing 柱填充

The resin utilized for chromatography is loaded into the column in a controlled manner to ensure a uniform distribution while preventing the formation of channels that will affect the performance of the unit operation. Commonly, a slurry containing resin in a process buffer is poured into the column. Once the resin is settled, the integrity of the packaged column is confirmed. In the case of reprocessing, the integrity of the column bed should be verified and confirmed prior to its use. Any issue affecting the bed should be solved prior to reprocessing, considering resuspension and repacking of the resin if applicable.

6.2.2 Cleaning and Sanitization 清洗與消毒

Full cleaning and sanitization of the column must be conducted in preparation for reprocessing. Cleaning and sanitization will follow existing procedures and practices, including the regeneration of the resin. (These elements are discussed further in (68, 69).)

6.2.3 Performance 操作性能

Performance of the chromatography step must be monitored according to the routine established procedures and must satisfy predefined acceptance criteria. The criteria should include, but not be limited to, the operational conditions (e.g., asymmetry, height equivalent to the theoretical plate, and/or transition analysis) and quality attributes (65).

6.2.4 Regeneration and Lifecycle 再生與生命週期

The resin must be regenerated consistent with established procedures and must satisfy the acceptance criteria defined and validated. The use of the resin for a reprocessing activity will be within the validated number of reuses if the reprocessing activity is not associated with a malfunction of the chromatography column and resin.

6.2.5 Validation and Filings 驗證與法規申報

Validation of reprocessing will be performed under a prospective protocol. Detailed guidance for validation activities of chromatography processes for the purification of proteins is provided in PDA TR 14 (68). In the event that changes are required to an existing filing, guidance is provided in PDA Technical Report No. 38: Manufacturing Chromatography Systems Post-Approval Changes (ChromPAC).

In this example, a protocol for prospective validation of reprocessing at the manufacturing scale was written and approved; however, the potential of a concurrent validation could be considered if the frequency for reprocessing did not justify a prospective protocol. The protocol required a single GMP run at manufacturing scale, including all routine in-process and release testing as well as additional nonroutine testing, for example, analysis of HCP, acidic variants, aggregate levels, fragmentation, oxidation, and potency in reprocessed material. The protocol also required placing the resulting drug substance in the stability program. The protocol acceptance criteria for nonroutine testing were based on the comparability criteria established in Section 6.4.3 and demonstrated at small-scale. (See Section 6.5.6.)

Yet, a full prospective validation approach may not be feasible or practical for reprocessing in all cases. Instead, a concurrent validation strategy may be more appropriate, allowing the manufacture and testing of products and only reprocessing when and if necessary. In the case of concurrent validation, the acceptance criteria shall be aligned with the approved specifications for the process.

The initial BLA to the FDA and MAA to the EMA for this new biologic included a complete manufacturing process development section for the AEX unit operation within Section 3.2.S.2.6 of the CTD. A comparability protocol was provided post-licensure to gain agreement with FDA on the implementation strategy and to request a reduction in reporting requirements from a PAS to a CBE-30 (i.e., documentation of changes being effected, 30-day response from FDA required). In the EU MAA, a Change Management Protocol was included that also outlined the implementation strategy to seek a reduction in reporting requirements from a Type II Variation to a Type IB Variation upon successful completion of the protocol.

Table 6.2.5-1 details the content required to support this type of regulatory strategy. The approach described is primarily focused on the U.S. and EU regulatory authorities that have defined regulatory pathways for this type of submission; however, the information described is also useful for regulatory filings in other countries.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

五大考量要點（6.2.1–6.2.5）決定再處理技術可行性：

  • 6.2.1 Column Packing（柱填充）：再處理前必須重新確認柱床（column bed）完整性。常用指標：HETP（Height Equivalent to Theoretical Plate，理論板高當量）、Asymmetry（不對稱因子）、transition analysis（轉換分析）。柱床若出現裂縫或通道，再處理毫無意義。
  • 6.2.2 Cleaning/Sanitization（清洗/消毒）：NaOH（sodium hydroxide，氫氧化鈉）是最常用的樹脂 sanitization 試劑；清洗 SOP 必須完整執行，不能因「趕時間再處理」而縮短。
  • 6.2.3 Performance（性能）：柱效測試不只看外觀，必須符合預定接受標準。
  • 6.2.4 Regeneration/Lifecycle（再生/生命週期）：再處理使用次數必須計入已驗證的樹脂壽命（resin lifetime）。若再處理導致超過驗證使用次數，需額外驗證延壽。
  • 6.2.5 Validation/Filings（驗證/申報）：再處理本身是一個製程變更，需要驗證並依 CTD 結構提交。FDA（美國）對應 CBE-30/PAS；EMA（歐盟）對應 Type IB/Type II Variation。

公式與計算 Formula

HETP（理論板高當量）= L / N
  L = 柱長（cm）
  N = 理論板數（由峰寬計算）

Asymmetry（不對稱因子）= b / a
  a = 從峰頂垂線到前峰半峰寬
  b = 從峰頂垂線到後峰半峰寬
  接受標準通常：0.8 ≤ Asymmetry ≤ 1.5

再生使用計數規則：
  Total use count = Normal runs + Reprocessing runs
  必須 ≤ Validated lifetime（已驗證生命週期）

重點提示 Key Notes

Prospective vs Concurrent Validation（前瞻性 vs 同步驗證）：

  • Prospective（前瞻性）：事先設計、執行、取得數據後才放行。再處理頻率高時適用。本案例採用 1 批 GMP 規模確認批。
  • Concurrent（同步）：允許在驗證執行期間放行批次，適用於再處理頻率極低、難以累積足夠批次的情境。接受標準必須對應已核准規格。

監管申報等級：FDA PAS（Prior Approval Supplement，事前核准補充申請）> CBE-30（Changes Being Effected，30 天通知）。透過 Comparability Protocol 預先取得 FDA 同意，可在驗證完成後改用 CBE-30，大幅縮短商業化時程。

比喻說明 Analogy

6.2.5 的監管策略就像先向主管機關「預告」一個工程變更計畫：「我打算在特定條件下執行再處理，以下是我的驗證方案和接受標準，請提前審核並同意未來改用簡化申報程序。」這樣當再處理真正發生時，只需遞交 CBE-30（30 天通知），而不必等待 PAS 的 6–12 個月審查，避免產品斷貨。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 若一根 AEX 樹脂的驗證壽命是 200 次，已正常使用 185 次，現在需要再處理 1 次，是否符合 6.2.4 的要求？如果需要第 2 次再處理呢？
  2. 在 EMA 框架下，Type II Variation 與 Type IB Variation 的主要差異是什麼？Change Management Protocol 如何幫助降低申報等級？

Table 6.2.5-1: Regulatory Submission Content 法規申報內容架構

6.3 Scope of Reprocessing 再處理範疇

原文內容 Original Text

6.3.1 Determining the Need for Reprocessing 確定再處理的必要性

Table 6.3.1-1 describes the scoring criteria for prospectively assessing the potential need for reprocessing in the hypothetical A-Mab process using an FMEA approach. The FMEA assesses the severity and detection of CQAs and how readily they are detected during unit operations. Scores are determined for Sections 6.5.2– 6.5.5 and Sections 6.4.1–6.4.3 according to the criteria below.

See Table 6.3.1-1 (FMEA Scoring Criteria) and Table 6.3.1-2 (FMEA Application Example 1) below.

The AEX chromatography step was operated in the flow-through mode, binding impurities such as DNA, HCP, endotoxin, and viruses to the resin while the antibody passed through. In addition, this step was designed to reduce levels of aggregate and acidic variants. Within the operating parameters of the AEX step, in this example, high levels of HCP in the column effluent are possible on rare occasions, and therefore, HCP is the quality attribute most likely to trigger reprocessing.

The risk assessment identified the AEX column (Table 6.3.1-2) as the step with the highest RPN. Development data indicated that the risk of high HCP levels was an inherent process risk and a rare event attributable to multiple, interacting sources of variability in the unit operation. Thus, the conclusion was that the AEX unit operation was a candidate for reprocessing.

The assigned scores are multiplied together (S × O × D = RPN) to determine the risk priority number (RPN). For example, for the "anion exchange chromatography" reprocessing step in Table 6.3.1-2, S × O × D = 5 × 5 × 5 = 125.

"Note: For HCP limits in Table 6.3.1-2: an appropriate IPC limit for DS HCP would typically be set at 70–80% of the action limit (approximately 70–80 ng/mg; a practical choice is 80 ng/mg). This provides a buffer to account for assay variability and process drift, enabling corrective actions before reaching the <100 ng/mg action limit."

6.3.2 Business Case and Project Charter 商業案例與專案章程

Three options were considered in assessing the business case for reprocessing at the AEX step:

  1. Discarding the batch upon failure to meet the HCP in-process control requirement of ≤80 ng/mg
  2. Redesigning the AEX step or adding additional steps
  3. Reprocessing during the AEX step

From a business perspective, it was confirmed that all three options could be managed to ensure acceptable product quality at release, but Option 3 was the most cost-effective and could be designed to meet quality and regulatory requirements. A project charter was created, and a cross-functional team was formed to develop a reprocessing step.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

FMEA（Failure Mode and Effects Analysis，失效模式與影響分析）：一種前瞻性的結構化風險評估工具，ICH Q9(R1) 推薦方法之一。三個評分維度：

  • S — Severity（嚴重性）：評估失效對 CQA 的潛在影響程度（1/3/5 三級）
  • O — Occurrence（發生頻率）：評估失效模式的發生概率（1/3/5 三級）
  • D — Detection（可偵測性）：評估在步驟完成前能否及時偵測到失效（1/3/5 三級）

RPN = S × O × D，範圍 1–125（本案例三個維度均為最高分 5）。

IPC（In-Process Control，製程中管控）：本案例中 AEX eluate HCP 的 IPC 限度設定為 ≤80 ng/mg（action limit ≤100 ng/mg 的 80%），作為再處理觸發點的警戒值。

比喻說明 Analogy

FMEA 評分就像汽車定期保養的風險檢查表：技師會為每個零件評估「壞了有多嚴重（S）」× 「多容易壞（O）」× 「壞了能不能及時發現（D）」= 整體風險分數。剎車片壞了很嚴重（S=5）、長期不換容易磨損（O=5）、但有警示燈可以偵測（D=1），RPN = 25；而 AEX 步驟的 HCP 問題：嚴重（S=5）× 偶爾發生（O=5）× 無法在步驟完成前即時偵測（D=5）= RPN 125，是所有步驟中最高的，因此被選為再處理候選步驟。

公式與計算 Formula

FMEA 評分邏輯（本案例）：

AEX 步驟 HCP 問題：
  S = 5（HCP 超標 → 直接影響 CQA）
  O = 5（每 <100 批中發生 1 次）
  D = 5（AEX eluate 無法在步驟完成前偵測 HCP）
  RPN = 5 × 5 × 5 = 125  ← 最高分，確認為候選步驟

對比：Protein A 步驟：
  S = 3, O = 1, D = 1 → RPN = 3（低風險）

對比：CEX 步驟：
  S = 5, O = 3, D = 1 → RPN = 15（中等風險）

IPC 觸發點設計：
  Action limit：HCP <100 ng/mg
  IPC alert limit：≤80 ng/mg（= action limit × 80%）
  → 80 ng/mg 超標 → 觸發再處理調查

重點提示 Key Notes

D = 5（無法偵測）是 AEX 選為再處理步驟的關鍵：HCP 需要專門的分析方法（ELISA 或 LC-MS），無法在製程中即時監控，只能在步驟完成後採樣分析。這就是為什麼 D = 5，也是為什麼需要預先設計再處理方案，而不是等到問題發生再臨時應對。

三選項決策框架：品質（CQA 合規性）是所有選項的前提，在三個選項都能確保產品品質的情況下，Option 3（再處理）因成本最低且不需要製程重新開發，成為首選。決策層級：CQA → Business。

實務應用 Practical Application

作為 CDMO，在與 Sponsor 或 DS CMO 進行技術轉移審查時，若 Sponsor 的 DS 製程包含 AEX 步驟，可以主動詢問：「是否已有再處理的 FMEA 評估？HCP 的 IPC alert limit 設定在何處？再處理觸發條件是否已寫入 BLA/MAA？」這展示了 CDMO 對上游製程的深度理解，有助於建立信任。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 如果 Virus-Retentive Filtration 步驟的 RPN = 25（S=5, O=5, D=1），為什麼不選它作為再處理候選步驟？（提示：考慮 D 值的含義）
  2. 為什麼 IPC alert limit 要設定在 action limit 的 70–80%（如 80 ng/mg），而不是直接用 100 ng/mg 作為觸發點？

Table 6.3.1-1: FMEA Scoring Criteria FMEA 評分標準

Scoring Category 評分類別 Score 1（低） Score 3（中） Score 5（高）
Severity (S) 嚴重性
Scored based on the potential of the failure to adversely affect a critical quality attribute		 Will not affect a CQA
（不影響 CQA）		 May lead to an effect on a CQA
（可能影響 CQA）		 Will lead to an effect on a CQA, possibly resulting in CQA failure
（將導致 CQA 失效）
Occurrence (O) 發生頻率
Scored based on the probability of the failure mode occurring		 1 in >1000 batches
（每千批以上 1 次）		 1 in 100 to 1000 batches
（每百至千批 1 次）		 1 in <100 batches
（每百批以內 1 次）
Detection (D) 可偵測性
How readily the failure mode could be detected prior to completion of the step		 Can readily detect
（可即時偵測）		 Indirect ability to detect
（間接偵測能力）		 Cannot readily detect
（無法即時偵測）

RPN (Risk Priority Number，風險優先數) = S × O × D，範圍 1–125。RPN 越高，優先級越高，越需要採取再處理或其他控制措施。

Table 6.3.1-2: Application of FMEA to the AEX Reprocessing Step (Example 1) FMEA 應用於 AEX 再處理步驟（範例一）

Reprocessing Step 製程步驟 S S Comments O O Comments D D Comments RPN
Protein A Chromatography
（Protein A 親和層析）		 3 HCP may be affected by loading and elution pH. 1 Based upon manufacturing experience, pH or loading excursions outside the normal operating range (NOR) may occur in 1 of >1000 batches. 1 Automated process control skids and batch record checks would readily detect a CPP excursion. 3
Low pH Inactivation
（低 pH 病毒滅活）		 5 Aggregation and viral inactivation may be affected by the pH, temperature, and time. 1 Based upon manufacturing experience, pH or loading excursions outside the NOR may occur in 1 of >1000 batches. 1 Batch record checks would readily detect a CPP excursion. 5
Cation Exchange Chromatography
（CEX，陽離子交換層析）		 5 Aggregate and HCP may be affected by loading, load/wash conductivity, elution pH, and elution collection. 3 Based upon manufacturing experience, excursions outside the NOR may occur in 1 of 100–1000 batches. 1 Automated process control skids and batch record checks would readily detect a CPP excursion. 15
Anion Exchange Chromatography
（AEX，陰離子交換層析）⭐ 最高 RPN		 5 HCP removal may be impacted by equilibrium/wash conductivity and load pH within the NOR. High conductivity and low pH are maximum challenge conditions. 5 Variability in this chromatography step occasionally leads to reduced HCP removal in 1 in <100 batches. 5 Failing levels of HCP at this step would not be detected. 125

（小病毒截留過濾）— 完整性失效		 5 An integrity failure of the virus retentive filter would impact the viral safety claim. 5 Based upon manufacturing experience, integrity test failures will occur in 1 of 50 virus filters. 1 Integrity testing of the virus retentive filters will identify a failure mode. 25
Small-virus Retentive Filtration
（小病毒截留過濾）— CPP 超限		 5 Exceeding a CPP limit would impact the viral safety claim. 3 Based upon manufacturing experience, overloading errors will occur in 1 of 100 batches. 1 Automated process control skids would readily detect a CPP excursion. 15
Formulation: Ultrafiltration/Diafiltration (UF/DF)
（配方：超濾/透濾）		 5 Product concentration will be affected by drug substance final dilution. Reconcentration may be required. 3 Based upon manufacturing experience, dilution errors will occur in 1 of 100 batches. 1 Concentration testing of the preformulated bulk will identify a failure mode. 15

RPN = S × O × D。AEX 步驟 RPN = 125（最高），確認為優先再處理候選步驟。NOR = Normal Operating Range（正常操作範圍）；CPP = Critical Process Parameter（關鍵製程參數）。

6.4 Quality Considerations 品質考量

原文內容 Original Text

6.4.1 Quality Attribute Impact Assessment 品質屬性影響評估

A risk analysis was performed to assess the effect of repeating the AEX chromatography step on the quality attributes (Table 6.4.1-1). The potential effect of the reprocessing step on both drug substance and intermediate quality attributes was assessed. For all quality attributes listed, it is assumed that the company has previously developed analytical techniques able to detect each, resulting in Detectability scores of 1. Attributes impacted by the AEX step were identified and included in Table 6.4.1-1. Attributes with an RPN ≥ 15 were identified for further evaluation.

See Table 6.4.1-1 (FMEA Application Example 2) below.

6.4.2 Analytical Methods 分析方法

In addition to routine drug substance release-testing, additional nonroutine analytical tests were identified as necessary for the development and implementation of reprocessing. In this case, an analysis of HCP, acidic variants, aggregate levels, fragmentation, oxidation, and potency in reprocessed material was performed during reduced-scale development studies. All of these characterization assays were either validated or qualified as appropriate for use with samples from the AEX eluate.

The same analytical methods performed during the laboratory-scale models were planned for subsequent full-scale verification runs (comparability protocol). In addition to routine release and stability-testing, the same nonroutine testing performed on AEX eluate in laboratory-scale models would be performed at manufacturing scale.

See Table 6.4.2-1 (Analytical Methods Summary) below.

6.4.3 Comparability Criteria 可比性標準

For laboratory-scale models, the intermediate quality attributes had to remain consistent with AEX eluate that had not been reprocessed, with the exception of HCP, which was expected to be reduced by the reprocessing event.

For manufacturing-scale studies, all drug substance release specifications continued to be met. Additionally, the intermediate quality attributes remained consistent with AEX eluate that had not been reprocessed, with the exception of HCP, which was expected to be reduced by the reprocessing event.

Drug substance from the first reprocessed batch was placed on the established real-time and accelerated stability protocols. It was determined that evaluation of the resulting drug product stability was not required.

6.4.4 Monitor Triggers 監控觸發點

The company continued to monitor the HCP in-process control test (action limit <100 ng/mg) at AEX eluate. (See Section 6.5.2.)

6.4.5 Investigate, Execute Protocols, Analyze Data, Document Results, and Complete Commitments 調查、執行方案、分析數據、記錄結果及履行承諾

Should the trigger described in Section 6.4.4 be reached, the event would prompt the company to investigate, execute protocols, analyze data, document results, and complete commitments. In all cases where reprocessing occurred, an investigation would be conducted evaluating the root cause, product quality impact, and corrective actions.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

6.4.1 第二輪 FMEA（Example 2）— 評估再處理本身對 CQA 的影響：與 6.3.1 的 FMEA（評估哪個步驟需要再處理）不同，6.4.1 的 FMEA 專門評估「如果執行 AEX 再處理，每個品質屬性會受到什麼影響」。由於假設公司已有完整分析方法，D = 1（均可偵測）。

RPN ≥ 15 的屬性需要進一步評估：包括 Protein concentration（蛋白質濃度）、Aggregate（聚集體）、Acidic variants（酸性異構體）、Fragmentation（碎片）、Potency（效力）、Oxidation（氧化）、HCP（宿主細胞蛋白）。這些屬性在 6.4.2 的分析方法中均需有對應檢測方法。

Comparability Criteria（可比性標準）：再處理後的中間品品質屬性必須與未再處理的 AEX eluate 「一致（consistent）」，唯一例外是 HCP——預期 HCP 水平因再處理而降低（這正是再處理的目的）。

重點提示 Key Notes

6.4.2 分析方法矩陣的深度：Table 6.4.2-1 涵蓋從聚集體（SEC、RP-HPLC、Fluorimetry）到糖基化（LC-MS、HPLC）的完整分析工具箱。非常規測試（nonroutine testing）需要在 AEX eluate 基質（matrix）中驗證（validated）或確認（qualified），不能直接借用 DS release 方法。

6.4.3 穩定性計畫：再處理的第一批 DS 必須納入已建立的實時穩定性（real-time stability）和加速穩定性（accelerated stability）方案。穩定性數據是後續 CBE-30/Type IB 提交的重要組成部分（見 Table 6.2.5-1，3.2.S.7）。

6.4.4 監控觸發機制設計原則：Action limit（動作限度）<100 ng/mg，alert limit（警戒限度）≤80 ng/mg（20% 緩衝帶，用於考慮分析變異度和製程漂移）。觸發點必須明確寫入 SOP 和批次記錄，確保 GMP 可追溯性。

6.4.5 調查義務（CAPA）：每次觸發再處理都必須進行正式調查，記錄根本原因（root cause）、對產品品質的影響評估（quality impact assessment）和糾正預防措施（CAPA）。這是 GMP 合規的基本要求，不能省略。

比喻說明 Analogy

6.4 的品質考量就像醫院的急救流程設計：在病人真正送達之前（= 再處理真正發生之前），醫院已預先設計好「哪些生命徵象需要監控（6.4.4）」、「哪些數值超標就啟動緊急程序（6.4.4 觸發點）」、「緊急手術的標準做法是什麼（6.4.5 執行方案）」、「手術後如何確認病人恢復正常（6.4.3 可比性標準）」。這種前瞻性設計讓真正的緊急事件發生時，每個人都知道該做什麼。

公式與計算 Formula

6.4.1 FMEA Example 2 關鍵數字：
  所有屬性 D = 1（假設均可偵測）
  RPN ≥ 15 → 需進一步評估

  Leachables/Extractables：S=3, O=3, D=3 → RPN=27
  （是唯一 D≠1 的項目，因第二次接觸樹脂/過濾器）

  Buffer/Solution supply：S=5, O=5, D=1 → RPN=25
  Equipment cleaning：S=5, O=5, D=1 → RPN=25
  （兩者為操作層面的風險，非品質屬性風險）

HCP 監控觸發設計：
  Release spec：<12 ng/mg（DS 放行規格）
  Action limit：<100 ng/mg（AEX eluate IPC）
  Alert limit：≤80 ng/mg（= 100 × 80%）
  再處理觸發：HCP >100 ng/mg → 啟動調查 + 再處理方案

實務應用 Practical Application

若 CDMO 負責 DP 端（Fill-Finish），而 Sponsor 的 DS CMO 執行了 AEX 再處理，CDMO 需要確認：(1) Sponsor 已按 6.4.3 完成可比性評估，DS 放行規格全部符合；(2) Sponsor 提供了正式調查報告（根本原因 + CAPA）；(3) 穩定性計畫包含再處理批次。這些是 DS/DP 介面品質協議（Quality Agreement）中應明確規定的 Sponsor 義務。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 在 6.4.1 的 FMEA 中，Leachables and Extractables 的 D 值為 3（非 1），這是什麼原因？在再處理設計中如何降低這個風險？
  2. 6.4.3 說「HCP 預期會降低（expected to be reduced）」——這是再處理的預期效果。如果再處理後 HCP 反而升高，應如何解讀？這批批次可以放行嗎？
  3. 6.4.5 要求每次再處理都要進行調查。調查應包含哪些必要元素，才能滿足 PIC/S GMP 的要求？

本節重點回顧 Section Summary (Part A: 6.0–6.4)

  • 6.0 框架定位：AEX 再處理案例是 TR74 最複雜的示範情境，刻意設計以涵蓋完整的再處理分析框架。品質管理系統、法規要求、製程理解是設計驅動力，商業考量排第三。
  • 6.1 單元操作理解：AEX 以 flow-through 模式清除 HCP/DNA/病毒，mAb 直接通過。系統組件（buffer reservoirs、pumps、column、resin、valves、sensors、controller）共同確保層析系統的可靠性。
  • 6.2 技術可行性評估五要點：柱填充完整性（6.2.1）→ 清洗/消毒（6.2.2）→ 性能測試（6.2.3）→ 樹脂壽命管理（6.2.4）→ 驗證與申報策略（6.2.5）。每個要點都是「再處理可以執行」的先決條件。
  • 6.3 FMEA Example 1（步驟層面）：AEX 步驟 RPN = 125（S=5, O=5, D=5），是所有純化步驟中唯一同時具有高嚴重性、高發生頻率、高不可偵測性的步驟，因此被確認為再處理候選步驟。三選項中，Option 3（再處理）在確保品質的前提下最具成本效益。
  • 6.4 FMEA Example 2（屬性層面）+ 品質把關機制：再處理對 Protein concentration、Aggregates、Acidic variants、Fragmentation、Potency、Oxidation、HCP 均可能有影響（RPN ≥ 15），需用 Table 6.4.2-1 的完整分析方法矩陣進行評估。可比性標準（6.4.3）、監控觸發點（6.4.4，HCP >100 ng/mg）和調查義務（6.4.5）形成完整的品質閉環。
  • 決策層級：CQA 合規性 → 業務可行性（Business Case）→ 操作執行（Project Charter）。品質永遠是第一道關卡。
PDA Technical Report No. 74 (Revised 2026) | Part B covers 6.5 Process Considerations & 6.6 Conclusions

本章學習目標

  • 理解 AEX 再處理步驟的設計與執行流程，包括從開發歷史回顧到製造移轉的完整路徑
  • 掌握 Reprocessing Trigger（再處理觸發條件）的設計邏輯，以及 IPC 測試如何作為再處理決策的客觀依據
  • 評估 Scaled-Down Model（縮小比例模型）在再處理驗證中的適用性，以及何時需要全規模確認批次
  • 了解如何透過雙重再處理（Double Reprocessing）作為最壞情境挑戰，建立保守的安全裕度
  • 體認 6.6 結論的核心訊息：再處理在技術上可行，但必須以嚴謹的開發工作與文件管理作為基礎
6.5 Process Considerations 製程考量

原文內容 Original Text

6.5 Process Considerations encompasses the full design-and-execute phase for an AEX reprocessing procedure, from revisiting original development data through to technology transfer into manufacturing. Eleven sub-sections (6.5.1–6.5.11) walk through each stage of a disciplined, risk-based development programme.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

Process Considerations（製程考量）：這一大節是整個 Appendix I 的執行核心。 前面的 6.3–6.4 完成了風險評估與品質屬性評估；6.5 則負責將這些分析轉化為 可執行的再處理程序，並驗證其有效性。

PPQ 思維（製程性能資格）：6.5 的整體架構與 Process Performance Qualification (PPQ) 的邏輯高度一致——先在縮小比例模型確認設計， 再在全規模進行確認性批次。

決策層次 Decision Hierarchy

在 6.5 所有設計決策中，優先順序不變：

  1. 無菌保證 Sterility Assurance
  2. 產品 CQA（HCP、Aggregate、病毒去除能力）
  3. 商業可行性（成本、時程）
6.5.1 Development History 開發歷史回顧

原文內容 Original Text

The development history of the AEX-column step should be reviewed to understand the purpose(s) of the original unit operation and the proposed reprocessing step. Control of CQAs and the potential impact to subsequent processing steps should be examined. Development studies that should be repeated or augmented to support reprocessing should be identified and discussed as described in Sections 6.5.2–6.5.4.

When considering a step for reprocessing, the original criticality assessment (Table 6.5.1-1) and an understanding of the original design parameters (Table 6.5.1-2) served as the technical basis for the design of the reprocessing procedure described in Section 6.5.3.

See Table 6.5.1-1 and Table 6.5.1-2 below (full-width).

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

Development History Review（開發歷史回顧）：不是重新做實驗， 而是系統性翻閱原始 AEX 步驟的開發資料——多變量研究、病毒清除模組試驗、 製程範圍研究——判斷哪些資料可以直接沿用，哪些需要補充。

Table 6.5.1-1 列出 HCP Clearance 相關的 CPP 分類與可接受範圍； Table 6.5.1-2 則進一步提供各參數的支持資料來源與管控策略， 是設計再處理步驟的技術地基。

比喻說明 Analogy

這就像修繕一棟建築前，先翻閱原始建築圖紙，確認哪些承重牆不能動、 哪些隔間可以調整。省略這步驟直接動工，後果可能是結構崩塌。 AEX 再處理設計亦同：跳過開發歷史回顧，便可能誤判哪些 CPP 在第二次通過時 仍有保護能力。

重點提示 Key Notes

Table 6.5.1-1 中 Operating Flow Rate ≤450 cm/h 和 AEX Load Conductivity ≤15 mS/cm 均為 CPP。 這些上限在再處理設計（6.5.3）中必須維持不變——因為它們直接影響 HCP 的結合與去除效率。

圖表解讀 Table Analysis — Tables 6.5.1-1 & 6.5.1-2

兩張表格的關鍵訊息：AEX 步驟有 5 個 CPP（pH、蛋白載量、流速、電導度）， 這些在再處理設計中必須維持在驗證範圍內。 Table 6.5.1-2 額外揭示每個 CPP 背後的支持資料（多變量研究 vs 病毒清除模組試驗）， 以及管控方式（批次紀錄程序 vs 製程控制系統）， 為後續 6.5.8 開發研究提供明確目標。

6.5.2 Reprocessing Triggers 再處理觸發條件

原文內容 Original Text

Based on a review of the development history and the prior risk assessment, an HCP critical in-process test following the AEX step was designed and implemented to serve as the trigger for an investigation (i.e., if HCP is >100 ng/mg). The test results were available within eight (8) hours of sampling.

The requirement for this additional eight-hour hold time was considered when designing the reprocessing step, as described in Section 6.4.3 and Sections 6.5.6–6.5.9. The introduction of this IPC test was a permanent process change that affected all production batches and not just the reprocessed batches.

The investigation procedure was defined in an SOP. If the investigation confirmed the positive result, then the reprocessing step would be initiated.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

Reprocessing Trigger（再處理觸發條件）：再處理不是自動執行的， 必須由客觀的量化指標啟動。本案例中，觸發條件是 AEX 洗出液 HCP >100 ng/mg。 這個閾值在 6.5.8 中被縮小比例模型支持，也在 6.3 的 FMEA 分析中被識別為高風險失效模式。

永久性製程變更（Permanent Process Change）：新增 HCP IPC 測試並非只用於 再處理批次，而是所有批次都必須執行。這是一個重要的監管邏輯——再處理機制的建立， 同時強化了整體製程的品質監控。

比喻說明 Analogy

想像工廠在產線末端加裝一個金屬探測器：它不是只為了處理特定批次才開機， 而是對每一件產品都進行掃描。觸發警報後，才啟動特定的處理程序。 AEX 後的 HCP IPC 測試邏輯相同——常態監控，異常才啟動再處理。

重點提示 Key Notes

8 小時結果等待時間直接影響了 AEX 洗出液的保留時間設計。 6.5.4 因此要求將最長保留時間從 72 小時延長至 120 小時（增加 48 小時緩衝）， 需要另行進行保留時間研究（6.5.9.1）。 這是設計牽一髮動全身的典型案例。

6.5.3 Reprocessing Design 再處理設計

原文內容 Original Text

The design of the AEX reprocessing step took into consideration the issues described in Sections 6.3.1, 6.3.2, 6.5.1, and 6.5.2. Since the step operated in flow-through mode, the AEX eluate was considered to be suitable as a feed-stream for AEX reprocessing without any adjustments.

Prior development studies reviewed in Section 6.5.1 showed that all ranges for feed-stream conditions expected for the reprocessing operation were evaluated and shown to produce drug substance with acceptable quality. Studies for the reprocessing step demonstrated that the AEX column—after being stripped, cleaned, and re-equilibrated—would readily remove HCP to well below acceptable levels.

All other aspects of the design of the reprocessing step, including operating conditions, buffer solution, equipment sizes, and others were similar to the design of the original AEX step.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

Flow-Through Mode（流通模式）的優勢：AEX 以流通模式操作（抗體不結合於樹脂， 雜質結合），使得洗出液（eluate）本身就是合適的再進料（feed-stream）， 無需調整緩衝液或蛋白質濃度。這大大簡化了再處理設計。

相比之下，若為結合-洗脫模式（bind-and-elute），再進料則需重新調整 pH 與電導度， 設計複雜度遠高於此。

重點提示 Key Notes

再處理設計的成功關鍵在於：不改變原始 AEX 步驟的操作條件。 這意味著原有的驗證資料（CPP 範圍、病毒清除 LRF）仍然有效， 毋需從頭驗證所有參數，大幅降低法規申報的負擔。

Column 在兩次操作間須完整執行：Stripping → CIP → Re-equilibration。 這是樹脂管理（Resin Management）的核心要求，確保第二次進料時 HCP 結合容量已完全恢復。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 若 AEX 步驟改為結合-洗脫模式，再處理設計會增加哪些複雜度？ 需要新增哪些研究？
  2. AEX 柱在再處理前須完成 Strip/CIP/Re-equilibration， 這對批次週期時間（batch cycle time）有何影響？
6.5.4 Design Impact Assessment 設計影響評估

原文內容 Original Text

After completing the design of the reprocessing step, the broader impact of the design on manufacturing operations was assessed. Since the AEX is a flow-through step, no adjustment to the buffer composition was required. The protein concentration was expected to be 30% lower than the original feed-stream but still within acceptable limits. The AEX load concentration is not considered a CPP.

A summary of the design impact assessment is included in Table 6.4.1-1 in the "Other" category. The two most significant areas of concern identified were Buffer/Solution Supply and Equipment Cleaning.

The maximum hold time for AEX eluate had to be increased by 48 hours to allow for completion of the HCP IPC test and to complete preparation of equipment and buffers in the event that the reprocessing trigger occurred. An evaluation of the manufacturing-scale microbial hold studies supported the longer hold time.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

Design Impact Assessment（設計影響評估）：再處理設計完成後， 必須評估其對製造現場的連鎖影響。本案例揭示兩大實務挑戰：

  • Buffer/Solution Supply：再處理需要額外的緩衝液， 必須確認生產現場的緩衝液準備能力與備品量。
  • Equipment Cleaning：設備清洗週轉時間影響保留時間， 需同步確認現有清洗程序能在再處理觸發後及時完成。

比喻說明 Analogy

設計影響評估就像餐廳在原有菜單外新增一道菜後，必須評估： 廚房是否有足夠的食材備料（Buffer Supply）？ 清洗設備的時間是否允許（Equipment Cleaning）？ 否則新菜上線時，整個廚房的節奏可能會被打亂。

重點提示 Key Notes

蛋白質濃度降低 30%（因稀釋效應）雖低於原始進料， 但因為 AEX 載量濃度（Load Concentration）在此案例中屬非關鍵參數， 不影響 HCP 去除效能。這是一個重要的判斷：非所有參數變化都需要補充研究， 關鍵是先確認分類（CPP or not）。

保留時間從 ≤72 小時延長至 ≤120 小時，新增 48 小時是為了容納： HCP 測試（8 小時）+ 設備/緩衝液準備時間。

6.5.5 Reassess Criticality of Process Inputs 重新評估製程輸入的關鍵性

原文內容 Original Text

A risk analysis was also performed to assess the effect of repeating the AEX chromatography step on the criticality of process parameters in Table 6.4.1-1. For all parameters listed, it is assumed that the company has the ability to routinely detect an exceedance resulting in Detectability scores of 1.

The risk associated with one input process parameter (hold time at pH 7.5 in Table 6.5.5-1) was determined to require additional development work to support longer hold times. A selection of other process inputs unrelated to operating parameters (e.g., raw materials, equipment cleaning) was also included in the FMEA assessment.

See Table 6.5.5-1 below (full-width).

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

Reassess Criticality（重新評估關鍵性）：再處理是一個額外的操作步驟， 會改變某些製程參數的 Occurrence（發生率）與 Severity（嚴重性）。 因此必須以再處理的角度重新執行 FMEA—— 即使是原本被分類為「非關鍵」的參數，也可能因為再處理而升級。

重點提示 Key Notes

Table 6.5.5-1 的關鍵發現：Hold at pH 7.5 的 RPN = 15 （S=3, O=5, D=1），是唯一需要額外研究的參數。 因為再處理後保留時間延長（從 72 小時到最多 120 小時）， 蛋白質在此 pH 下停留更長時間，潛在影響 Aggregate、Deamidation 等 CQA， Occurrence 分數因此升至 5。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 為何 Table 6.5.5-1 中大多數 CPP（AEX load pH、Protein load 等）的 RPN 均為 5， 而非 15 或更高？提示：思考 Occurrence 分數為何設定為 1。
  2. 如果「Protein concentration in load」從 Noncritical 改分類為 CPP， 對再處理設計會有何影響？
